PMP Exam 5
Question 1 of 200
Question ID: 612224
You have data about the top five causes of flight delays that occurred over the past three years,
including how many minutes each flight varied from being on time, both early and late. For a list
of causes, you have the frequency each cause occurred. You also have enough data about
multiple causes for each flight delay to find correlations between factors.
Which of the following quality tools would help you the most to identify the causes leading to
the highest number of delays?
- **A Scatter diagram**
- **B Control chart**
- **C Histogram**
- **D Cause-and-effect diagram**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which tool helps in displaying data about the frequency of factors or causes?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

According to the scenario provided, you are carrying out the Manage Quality process. A
histogram is an example of the data representation technique that can be used during this process.
- **A histogram is a vertical bar chart that shows a graphical representation of numerical data. The**
question is asking you to focus on the most significant causes. You have the data to display the
causes and rank them based on the frequency they occur to identify the vital few causes
responsible for most of your delays, thus making the histogram the best answer to the question
asked. Additionally, the causes can be sorted by their frequency to identify the top cause(s). This
sorting turns the simple histogram into what is called a Pareto chart.
Although it is not mentioned in the current edition of the PMBOK® Guide, the Pareto chart is a
type of histogram that displays causes, sorted so the most frequent causes are first, which helps

---

you prioritize what will give you the best return on investment in addressing the top causes. For
example, potential categories may include causes such as 'weather', 'mechanical issues', 'security',
'other'. The corresponding bars are then plotted on the horizontal axis in descending order of
magnitude starting with the source that most frequently contributes to the flight delays and going
down to the source, such as 'other', that has the least number of occurrences. Then, the Pareto
principle of 80/20 can be applied to focus on the most significant 20% sources that contribute to
the 80% of the flight delays.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Scatter diagram**
Incorrect. A scatter diagram is a graph that shows the relationships between two variables,
while in the scenario, you have multiple causes that resulted in flight delays. Additionally,
the scatter diagram does not help you focus on the most significant cause.
- **B Control chart**
Incorrect. Control charts are used to show whether a process is stable or not. The data you
have allows you to determine how many minutes each flight varied from being on time for
the last five years, both early and late. However, although a control chart shows variances
in such values, it does not focus on the most significant cause.
- **C Histogram**
Correct. A histogram is a vertical bar chart that can show the number of defects per
deliverable, a ranking of the cause of defects, the number of times each process is
noncompliant, or other representations of project or product defects. To rank the causes,
you can use the data you have on the frequency each occurred.
- **D Cause-and-effect diagram**
Incorrect. A cause-and-effect diagram, also known as an Ishikawa diagram or fishbone
diagram, is used to find the root cause of a problem. However, a cause-and-effect diagram
does not focus on the frequency of the causes.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 293; see
also http://asq.org/learn-about-quality/cause-analysis-tools/overview/pareto.html

---

PMP Exam 5
Question 2 of 200
Question ID: 613024
- **A team member working in a matrix organization has produced two major deliverables that**
failed to meet the quality specifications. The project coordinator tried to clear up
misunderstandings about the specifications, but the quality issues persisted. The project
coordinator approached the employee's functional manager to help resolve the problem.
What kind of power is the project coordinator asking the functional manager to invoke?
- **A Persuasive**
- **B Expert**
- **C Coercive**
- **D Legitimate**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project coordinator is escalating this issue to a functional manager who serves as the
superior of the poor performing team member.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Positional (also known as formal, authoritative, and legitimate) power is based on formal
position granted in the hierarchy of the organization, or the authority granted by the project
charter. This is the kind of power you can use when assigning work to someone who reports to
you. According to the scenario described, the project team is working for a company structured
as a matrix organization. A functional manager has more legitimate authority in a matrix
organization than a project coordinator. Therefore, by turning to the functional manager, the
project coordinator is invoking legitimate power.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Persuasive**
Incorrect. Persuasive power uses arguments or rhetoric that motivate people to a desired
course of action. This situation does not have evidence of the project coordinator using
persuasive arguments.
- **B Expert**
Incorrect. Expert power is indirectly used in this scenario when the project coordinator
asks the poor performing team member to meet with a more skillful peer to clear up
misunderstandings about the quality specifications. However, turning to the functional
manager does not invoke the authority of skill, training, experience, certification, or
information possessed that is inherent in expert power.
- **C Coercive**
Incorrect. Coercive or punitive power uses an explicit threat of disciplinary measures and
negative consequences. The functional manager may have such authority including official
censure, docking pay, or firing, but the act of turning to the functional manager does not
create the immediate threat.
- **D Legitimate**
Correct. Legitimate power, also called positional, formal, or authoritative, is granted due
to the person's selection or appointment to their position in the organization or hierarchy. A
functional manager has the authority to invoke other powers such as referent, expert,
reward, or coercive.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 63
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Question 3 of 200
Question ID: 612114
You are assisting a project sponsor with the development of a document, which authorizes a
product development project. Currently, you need to identify the project's key deliverables for
inclusion in the document.
What might you do to obtain this information?
- **A Ask the project sponsor for a copy of the project charter**
- **B Research the company's organizational process assets**
- **C Invite the project sponsor and other key stakeholders to join a conference call**
- **D Look at the project scope statement**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

You, as the project manager, are assisting the project sponsor with the development of the project
charter.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project charter is the document that is being developed. The project
charter is a document issued by the project initiator or sponsor that formally authorizes the
existence of a project and provides the project manager with the authority to apply organizational
resources to project activities. The project charter is created as an output of the Develop Project
Charter process. Meetings are one of the tools and techniques that may be used during the
Develop Project Charter process, and a conference call is a type of meeting. During the Develop
Project Charter process, meetings may be held with key stakeholders to identify the project
objectives, success criteria, key deliverables, high-level requirements, summary milestones, and
other summary information. The incorrect answer choices represent sources of information that
are not yet available at this point in the project or would not have the needed information.
Therefore, of the available choices, the best way for you, as the project manager, to obtain

---

information on the project's key deliverables is to invite the project sponsor and other key
stakeholders to join a conference call.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Ask the project sponsor for a copy of the project charter**
Incorrect. The question suggests that the project charter is the document that the project
manager is developing. Therefore, the project charter is not yet available to be used as a
resource.
- **B Research the company's organizational process assets**
Incorrect. The question describes the project charter as the document under development.
The organizational process assets (OPAs) may have a template that can be used to develop
the project charter. However, the OPAs are not likely to list the key deliverables for a
project in the initiation stage.
- **C Invite the project sponsor and other key stakeholders to join a conference call**
Correct. A conference call is an example of a meeting. During the Develop Project Charter
process, meetings may be held with key stakeholders to identify the project objectives,
success criteria, key deliverables, high-level requirements, summary milestones, and other
summary information.
- **D Look at the project scope statement**
Incorrect. The project scope statement is a description of the project scope, major
deliverables, assumptions, and constraints. The project scope statement is an output of the
Define Scope process, which is performed as part of the Planning Process Group, whereas
the question suggests that the Develop Project Charter process is underway, which is
conducted during the Initiating Process Group.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 80

PMP Exam 5
Question 4 of 200
Question ID: 612062
You are leading a software development project for a client. The change control board (CCB) has
been inundated with change requests from the client throughout the project as the product has
evolved. This situation drives the team crazy and makes controlling the project scope extremely
challenging and time-consuming.
Which of the following tailoring considerations might you have missed earlier in the project?
- **A Diversity**
- **B Stability of requirements**
- **C Physical location**
- **D Validation and control**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which tailoring consideration may have led you, as the project manager, to select a different
development approach?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question describes a situation where the client is continually changing the project
requirements as the product under development evolves. This situation is driving the client to
submit change requests, which must be reviewed by the change control board (CCB). Projects,
where the product under development is expected to evolve throughout the project, can be said to
have unstable requirements. The stability of requirements should be considered to determine the
appropriate development approach. In this case, it is apparent that the strict change control
processes and procedures of a traditional waterfall approach are not well suited to the needs of
the client who is forced to submit change requests as the product changes and evolves. In this
circumstance, an agile approach may have been more appropriate for the project. An agile
approach welcomes change and harnesses it for the customer's benefit. Had you, as the project
manager, considered the stability (or, in this case, instability) of the product requirements, you

---

may have selected an approach more appropriate for the project. For example, the project, at a
high level, could have still been lead using waterfall, but the actual development of the product
performed by the team could have been carried out using agile, thus making the whole project
hybrid.
Note, the development approach is also a tailoring consideration for the scope management
processes, but it was not offered as an answer choice. Therefore, of the available options, the
stability of requirements is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Diversity**
Incorrect. The diverse background of the team is an important consideration in resource
management, but it is not very relevant to controlling scope. Additionally, there is no
information presented by the question to suggest that a diversity issue exists in the project.
- **B Stability of requirements**
Correct. The stability of requirements should be considered to determine the appropriate
development approach. In this case, it is apparent that the change control requirements of a
traditional waterfall approach are not well suited to the needs of the client who is forced to
submit change requests as the product changes and evolves.
- **C Physical location**
Incorrect. Physical location is a tailoring consideration associated with the resource
management processes rather than the scope management processes. Additionally, the
physical location of team members and resources is not likely to create the problem of
excessive change requests.
- **D Validation and control**
Incorrect. There is no indication from the question of an issue with proper validation and
control procedures. The use of a change control board (CCB) in a waterfall approach is an
appropriate method of controlling the project's scope. In this case, the problem involves the
selected development approach driving excessive change requests rather than how those
change requests are being processed.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 133
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Question 5 of 200
Question ID: 613002
You are in the process of obtaining team members for the project you are managing. Some of the
selected individuals have existing obligations for other projects, which limits their availability
for your project.
What should you do to ensure that information about the availability of the team members is
documented?
- **A Capture the availability of the team members in the stakeholder register**
- **B Update the project schedule to reflect the team members' availability**
- **C Record the availability of the team members in the resource calendar**
- **D Request the human resources manager to update the resource breakdown structure**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where should you document the working days and shifts upon which each project team member
is available?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project team members are being selected as part of the Acquire
Resources process. One of the outputs of this process is the resource calendars. A resource
calendar identifies the working days, shifts, start and end of normal business hours, weekends,
and public holidays when each specific resource is available. Resource calendars also specify
when and for how long identified team and physical resources will be available during the
project. In this scenario, some of the selected project team members have availability limitations.
These limitations can be documented in the resource calendar. Therefore, recording the team
members' availability in the resource calendar is the best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Capture the availability of the team members in the stakeholder register**
Incorrect. The stakeholder register is a project document with the identification,
assessment, and classification of project stakeholders. Although the stakeholder register
should include the project team members, their availability is not part of this document.
- **B Update the project schedule to reflect the team members' availability**
Incorrect. Changes to the project schedule may result from the availability of the required
resources. However, the project schedule will only show when the project team members
are scheduled for project activities. It will not reflect the availability of the project team
members.
- **C Record the availability of the team members in the resource calendar**
Correct. The resource calendar is a calendar that identifies the working days and shifts
upon which each specific resource is available.
- **D Request the human resources manager to update the resource breakdown structure**
Incorrect. The resource breakdown structure is a hierarchical representation of resources
by category and type. However, the resource breakdown structure does not provide
information on resource availability. Additionally, it is unclear from the scenario if the
human resources manager is the one who is responsible to update the resource breakdown
structure for the project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 334

PMP Exam 5
Question 6 of 200
Question ID: 651317
As part of project activities, new equipment should be installed at a plant. The plant manager
informs the project manager that due to the nature of work, the installation of the equipment
must be done prior to hiring seasonal staff.
Which of the following statement is correct?
- **A There is a mandatory dependency between the hiring of seasonal staff and the equipment**
installation.
- **B There is an early finish date between the hiring of seasonal staff and the equipment**
installation.
- **C There is no dependency between what the project team is working on and the plant**
manager's operations.
- **D There is a discretionary dependency between the installation of the equipment and the**
hiring of seasonal staff.
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Does anything have to happen before anything else?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Dependency determination is among the tools and techniques that can be used as part of the
Sequence Activities process. In the scenario, the plant manager informs the project manager that
the installation of equipment must be done prior to the hiring of staff. That requirement makes
the dependency between these two activities as mandatory.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A There is a mandatory dependency between the hiring of seasonal staff and the equipment**
installation.
Correct. Mandatory dependencies are those that are legally or contractually required or
inherent in the nature of work. Based on the scenario described, installation of the
equipment ‘must’ happen prior to the hiring of the staff, as mandated by the plant manager.
- **B There is an early finish date between the hiring of seasonal staff and the equipment**
installation.
Incorrect. The early finish date is the earliest possible point in time when the uncompleted
portions of an activity can finish. There is no information in this question to set early finish
dates for the hiring of the staff and installation of the equipment activities.
- **C There is no dependency between what the project team is working on and the plant**
manager's operations.
Incorrect. Based on the scenario, there is at least one dependency - the installation of the
equipment and the hiring of seasonal staff.
- **D There is a discretionary dependency between the installation of the equipment and the**
hiring of seasonal staff.
Incorrect. Discretionary dependencies are those dependencies recommended by best
practices and inherent logic but not required. In this scenario, there is a required
dependency between two project activities or events.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 191-192
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Question 7 of 200
Question ID: 612213
- **A change request has been approved and is currently being implemented by the project team.**
According to the project life cycle shown on the chart below, which of the following is true about
project costs and risks associated with the process group described in this scenario?
- **A Both the cost of changes and the project risk are zero.**
- **B The cost of changes is lowest while the project risk is highest.**
- **C The cost of changes is nearly equal to project risk.**
- **D The cost of changes is highest while project risk is lowest.**
Question answered incorrectly

---


**Hint:**

Identify which process the project team is currently performing, map it to the appropriate process
group, and then determine what is true about this process group according to the generic life
cycle.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

All projects can be mapped to the generic life cycle consisting of five Process Groups: Initiating
takes place at the beginning of a project, then Planning, then Executing takes place in the middle,
and then the project ends with Closing. Processes of the Monitoring and Controlling Process
Group are carried out throughout the project. According to the project generic life cycle, the cost
of changes are about equal to project risks in the middle or late middle of the project. In the
scenario, the project team is currently implementing an approved change request. This activity is
undertaken in the Direct and Manage Project Work process, part of the Executing Process Group.
Since execution takes place approximately halfway into the project timeline where the curve
representing the cost of changes intersects with the curve representing the risk, it would be true
to say that the cost of changes is nearly equal with project risk.
If you are still not convinced, consider this: the lowest/highest values as far as the cost of
changes and risk are concerned, apply to the very beginning or end of the project. One moment
after the project has been initiated, the cost of changes is one tick higher than its lowest level,
and the risk is one tick lower than its highest level. Same applies to project closure: one moment
before the project is closed, the cost of changes is one tick lower than its highest level, and the
risk is one tick higher than its lowest level.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Both the cost of changes and the project risk are zero.**
Incorrect. Zero cost of changes and zero project risk can typically be encountered before
the processes of the Initiating Process Group take place. According to the scenario
described, the project team is implementing a change request, implying the project is in
execution. Therefore, this answer choice can be eliminated.
- **B The cost of changes is lowest while the project risk is highest.**
Incorrect. The cost of changes is lowest, and uncertainties highest, during the Planning
Process Group, before any work has begun. In the scenario, work has already begun,
making this choice an incorrect answer.

---

- **C The cost of changes is nearly equal to project risk.**
Correct. Since the cost of changes rises throughout the project, and risk decreases
throughout the project, their trend lines cross and are equal in the middle or late part of
project execution. According to the scenario, the project team is implementing an approved
change request. Since this activity takes place during the Direct and Manage Project Work
process that belongs to the Executing Process Group, this choice represents a true
statement and is, therefore, the best answer.
- **D The cost of changes is highest while project risk is lowest.**
Incorrect. The cost of changes is highest, and uncertainty lowest, at the end of the project,
during the Closing Process Group. Implementation of the approved change request
described in the question takes place in the Executing Process Group, making this choice
an incorrect answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 548-549, 90
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 8 of 200
Question ID: 651314
As your project has uncovered new methodologies to achieve results exceeding all expectations,
your team sees an opportunity to attach the project work to a larger initiative in the company
beyond the boundaries of the project. You and a few key team members present the idea with the
project sponsor and other executives.
Which risk strategy was used?
- **A Exploit**
- **B Transfer**
- **C Mitigate**
- **D Escalate**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Is this becoming bigger than your project alone?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

This question is asking, which risk strategy was used in this scenario. The PMBOK® Guide
describes five strategies for opportunities and five strategies for threats. The situation describes a
positive risk or opportunity, therefore mitigate and transfer strategies that apply to threats, are
incorrect choices.
An exploit strategy means that the project team ensures that the probability that a positive event
happens is 100%, so that corresponding benefits can be gained. When using an exploit strategy,
the risks still stays within the bounds of the current project scope in terms of response and
monitoring and controlling, which is not the case in this scenario.

---

The question describes an opportunity that goes beyond the project and outside of the project
manager’s scope of authority, in which case, the project manager and other key team members
notify the project sponsor and other executives. After escalation, the opportunity is not further
monitored by the project team. It is up to the project sponsors and other executives to take
advantage of the opportunity. Note that the escalate strategy applies not only to opportunities but
the threats as well.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Exploit**
Incorrect. Exploiting is a risk strategy aimed at taking advantage of a high priority
opportunity. This question describes an opportunity that lies outside of the scope and
normal boundaries of the project and the project manager's authority.
- **B Transfer**
Incorrect. Sharing or transferring moves the ownership of the risk to a third party. The
team in this question is not seeking to hand over ownership of the risk to an outside party,
but to extend the risk outside the bounds of the current project scope.
- **C Mitigate**
Incorrect. Mitigating is reducing the probability of occurrence or impact of the threat. It is
used for negative risks (threats). This is a positive risk (opportunity).
- **D Escalate**
Correct. Escalating extends the opportunity beyond the scope of the project to a much
broader and higher level. This is a result of the opportunity exceeding the project
manager’s authority.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 444
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 9 of 200
Question ID: 613319
Early in project execution, you obtain some of the equipment, materials, and supplies needed for
a project you are managing. Since you feel the acquisition of these resources was very efficient,
you want to ensure this best practice is available to the project stakeholders to improve the future
performance of the current project.
What is your best course of action?
- **A Document the best practice in the resource management plan**
- **B Begin project closure as the project objectives have been achieved**
- **C Add the knowledge gained to the enterprise environmental factors**
- **D Inform the procurement department's manager of the best practice**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

You, as the project manager, were performing the Acquire Resources process when the
knowledge was gained.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that you, as the project manager, were performing the Acquire Resources
process when knowledge which might improve the process of acquiring future resources was
gained. Updates to the project management plan, including its components such as the resource
management plan, are an output of this process. Updating the resource management plan to
include the best practice may improve future project performance. Therefore, of the available
options, documenting the best practice in the resource management plan is the best answer to the
question asked. Note, an approved change request is needed for the resource management plan to
be updated.

---

One may argue that updating the resource management with the actual experience in acquiring
project resources, especially if the acquisition went well, is not required since the resources have
been acquired according to the plan. While this may indeed be a plausible argument, the
reference specifically indicates that "The resource management plan may be updated to reflect
actual experience in acquiring resources for the project, including lessons learned in acquiring
resources early in the project that will impact how resources are acquired later in the project."
This description closely matches the situation described in the scenario, thus making the update
of the resource management plan the best answer to the question asked.
Another argument can be made that updating a lessons learned register would be a better answer.
While updating the lessons learned register could be a plausible choice, this answer is not
provided amongst the choices.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Document the best practice in the resource management plan**
Correct. Updating the resource management plan to include the best practice may improve
future project performance. An approved change request is needed before the plan can be
updated. While submitting the change request is not covered by this choice, of the options
provided, document the best practice in the resource management plan is still the best
answer to the question asked.
- **B Begin project closure as the project objectives have been achieved**
Incorrect. Nothing in the question suggests the project objectives have been achieved.
According to the scenario, the project has just begun its execution activities. Closing the
project is premature and makes little sense.
- **C Add the knowledge gained to the enterprise environmental factors**
Incorrect. While updates to the enterprise environmental factors (EEFs) are one of the
outputs of the Acquire Resources process implied by the scenario, EEFs typically refer to
conditions that influence, constrain, or direct the project rather than serve as a knowledge
base that can help improve the future performance of the current project as asked by the
question.
- **D Inform the procurement department's manager of the best practice**
Incorrect. The question does not indicate that the performing organization has a
procurement department. If a procurement department does exist, it may be a good idea to

---

inform them of the best practice. However, it is unlikely that this action will affect the
performance of the current project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 334
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 10 of 200
Question ID: 612066
- **A project manager has ongoing issues with a pre-qualified seller who has repeatedly failed to**
meet quality standards specified in the contract. The seller has also been unresponsive when the
project manager has tried to resolve the quality issues. The project manager wants to ensure that
this seller will not be considered again for future contracts.
What is the best course of action for the project manager to take in this situation?
- **A Remove the seller from the prequalified sellers list**
- **B Capture the information in the issue log**
- **C Update the project management plan**
- **D Conduct a procurement audit**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where do you find a list of preapproved sellers?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Control Procurements process is being performed, and one of the
organizational process assets associated with this process is prequalified seller lists. Prequalified
seller lists contain potential sellers who are previously qualified (approved). These lists can be
updated as an output of the Control Procurements process, and sellers can be disqualified and
removed from the lists based on poor performance, such as the one described in the scenario.
Therefore, of the choices provided, to ensure that this seller will not be considered again for
future contracts, removing the seller from the prequalified sellers list is the best course of action
for the project manager to take in this situation.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Remove the seller from the prequalified sellers list**
Correct. Prequalified seller lists is an organizational process asset, which contains
potential sellers who are previously qualified (approved). These lists can be updated
according to the Control Procurements process, and sellers can be disqualified and
removed from the lists based on their poor performance.
- **B Capture the information in the issue log**
Incorrect. While the issue should be captured in the issue log, this action will not prevent
the seller from bidding on future contracts.
- **C Update the project management plan**
Incorrect. A project management plan does not contain information regarding specific
sellers and would not prevent the seller from being selected for future projects.
- **D Conduct a procurement audit**
Incorrect. A procurement audit is a structured review of the procurement process. It does
not contain information about seller eligibility for contracts.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 501
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 11 of 200
Question ID: 612447
The project manager has gained the support of senior management who has committed to
providing the necessary funding to design and develop a prototype for a new initiative. The
project manager is working on creating the project charter and needs someone to serve as the
project sponsor.
Which of the following best meets the needs of the project manager?
- **A Project manager**
- **B Project management office (PMO)**
- **C Any project team member**
- **D Any person external to the project**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What person or entity can commit resources to initiate a project?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Projects are initiated by an entity external to the project such as a sponsor, project management
office (PMO), or a portfolio governing body chairperson or authorized representative. The
project initiator or sponsor should be at a level that is appropriate to procure funding and commit
resources to the project. Of the available choices, only the PMO is external to the project and has
the authority to allocate resources to initiate a project.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Project manager**
Incorrect. Projects are initiated by an entity external to the project; therefore, the project
manager is not eligible to serve as the project sponsor.
- **B Project management office (PMO)**
Correct. Projects are initiated by an entity external to the project such as a sponsor, project
management office (PMO), or a portfolio governing body chairperson or authorized
representative.
- **C Any project team member**
Incorrect. A project can be initiated by an entity external to the project. Therefore, not only
all project team members are excluded from serving as the project sponsor because they are
part of the project, but also it is unlikely that a project team member will be at a level that
is appropriate to procure funding and commit resources to the project.
- **D Any person external to the project**
Incorrect. While it is correct that an external entity is required to initiate a project, the
project initiator or sponsor should be at a level that is appropriate to procure funding and
commit resources to the project. Saying that ‘any’ person external to the project can initiate
the project would be too much of a generalization and is, therefore, not the best answer to
the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 77
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 12 of 200
Question ID: 613276
According to the industry's generally accepted best practices, the electrical work on the
appliances assembly line should be completed prior to installing the doors.
What does this sequence of activities represent?
- **A Activity attributes**
- **B Discretionary dependencies**
- **C Activity list**
- **D Mandatory dependencies**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What sequencing activity tool or technique is based on knowledge of an industry’s best
practices?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Use of the four attributes within the dependency determination and integration tool or technique
helps define the logical sequencing of the work to be performed as efficiently as possible as a
discretionary dependency. The process established is not mandatory, meaning not based on legal
or contractual requirements or any requirement unique to the appliance assembly itself, and as
such, the process could be re-ordered. However, using the sequencing order known to be the best
practice in the industry reduces the overall project risk.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Activity attributes**
Incorrect. The question references sequencing methodology and does not touch on the
extended descriptions of project activities that identify multiple components associated with
each activity, which is the description of activity attributes.
- **B Discretionary dependencies**
Correct. Discretionary dependencies are established based on knowledge of best practices
within a particular application area or some unusual aspect of the project where a specific
sequence is desired.
- **C Activity list**
Incorrect. The activity list is the project document that contains all schedule activities
required on the project that are to be sequenced. The activity list does not specify the order
in which the activities are to be performed.
- **D Mandatory dependencies**
Incorrect. Mandatory dependencies are those that are legally or contractually required or
inherent in the nature of the work. According to the scenario, the sequence of activities is
established based on the industry's generally accepted best practices which can be best
described as discretionary dependencies.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 191

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 13 of 200
Question ID: 612311
As a result of the customer inspection, the project manager realizes that some of the components
of the project management plan, such as the cost baseline, schedule baseline, and procurement
management plan, should be updated.
What should the project manager do next?
- **A Conduct a procurement audit**
- **B Update the components as necessary**
- **C Submit a change request**
- **D Begin the Close Project or Phase process**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is needed to update the project management plan when the project is in execution?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario describes a project where a customer has conducted an inspection which resulted in
a need to update some of the components of the project management plan. An inspection is one
of the tools and techniques of the Control Procurements process. This process can result in
change requests as one of its outputs. Changes can be requested to update the project
management plan, its subsidiary plans, and other components such as the cost baseline, schedule
baseline, and procurement management plan. Therefore, of the choices provided, under the
circumstances described in the scenario, submitting a change request is the best answer to the
question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Conduct a procurement audit**
Incorrect. An audit, as it pertains to the Control Procurements process implied by the
scenario, is a structured review of the procurement process. While conducting a
procurement audit is a good project management practice, this action does not address the
essence of the question which is about updating the components of the project management
plan as a result of the inspection carried out by the customer.
- **B Update the components as necessary**
Incorrect. According to the scenario, the project is in the Control Procurements process.
This means project planning has been completed and the project management plan
finalized. Updating the components of the project management plan for a project in
execution (onwards) cannot be done without an approved change request.
- **C Submit a change request**
Correct. The scenario implies the Control Procurements process is being performed. When
an update to the project management plan is required, a change request should be
submitted. If the change request is approved, the project management plan (or any of its
components) can then be updated.
- **D Begin the Close Project or Phase process**
Incorrect. Nothing in the question indicates the project is approaching its end. The scenario
implies the project is in execution, the customer has conducted an inspection, and the
project management plan should be updated. Starting the Close Project or Phase process is
premature.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 499

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 14 of 200
Question ID: 613265
The deliverables of a two-year-long project have just been accepted. It is four months late, but
the customer is pleased to have it. The project manager is glad to be done with the deliverables
but is concerned about the cost and schedule overruns. He decides to re-run the initial
cost-benefit analysis using the actual project costs.
Where should the project manager obtain the initial cost-benefit analysis?
- **A From the customer**
- **B The project charter**
- **C The business case**
- **D The benefits management plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

It is the document that justified the project.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

- **A business case contains a documented economic feasibility study used to establish the validity**
of the benefits of a selected component lacking sufficient definition and that is used as a basis for
the authorization of further project management activities. The business case has the complete
cost-benefit analysis for the project. It can provide the project manager with all the initial
information used to justify the project, allowing the project manager can re-run the cost-benefit
analysis substituting actual costs for the analysis.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A From the customer**
Incorrect. The question is taken from the perspective of the supplier. The customer will be
aware of the price charged by the supplier but will not likely have any relevant information
on the vendor's costs and cost-benefit analysis for the project. The data for a cost-benefit
analysis, including conditions that were known at the start of the project, are included in
the vendor's business documents.
- **B The project charter**
Incorrect. The project charter defines success criteria and other measurable objectives but
is not likely to have the complete cost-benefit analysis.
- **C The business case**
Correct. The business case has the complete cost-benefit analysis for the project. It can
provide the project manager with all the initial information used to justify the project.
- **D The benefits management plan**
Incorrect. The benefits management plan explains the processes for creating, maximizing,
and sustaining the benefits provided by a project or program. It outlines the benefits of all
projects and how they are to be maintained beyond the completion of the project. It does
not have the cost-benefit analysis.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 125

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 15 of 200
Question ID: 625213
You conduct a variance analysis on the project you manage and determine that additional work is
needed to complete the deliverables. You evaluate the impact and find that the additional work
will create a two-day delay. You meet with the stakeholders to inform them about the delay.
What other action should you take?
- **A Request additional funds**
- **B No additional action is needed.**
- **C Submit a change request**
- **D Review statement of work**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

This would require updating the project management plan elements that include the project scope
statement, WBS, WBS dictionary, and the approved version of a schedule model.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scope baseline is the approved version of a scope statement, work breakdown structure, and
the WBS dictionary. The scope baseline defines all the work required to be performed on the
project. The schedule baseline is the approved version of a schedule model. When additional
work is required to complete the project deliverables, the work should be documented in the
scope baseline. When the additional work causes the project schedule to be delayed, this delay
should be reflected in the schedule baseline. An update of both the scope baseline and the
schedule baseline would require an action; specifically, a change request submission through the
Perform Integrated Change Control process. Therefore, just informing the stakeholders that the
project will be delayed would not be enough. A change request should be submitted.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Request additional funds**
Incorrect. The question suggests that the additional work will cause a two-day delay. The
question does not provide any information on whether additional funds are required. If the
schedule delay is not approved, but instead additional resources are brought to the project
to complete the work within the original timeline, then additional funds may be required to
cover those resources. However, this determination should be done only after a change
request is submitted and processed through the Perform Integrated Change Control
process.
- **B No additional action is needed.**
Incorrect. When actual project performance is not aligned with the project management
plan, an action (corrective, preventive, or defect repair) is required.
- **C Submit a change request**
Correct. The work required to complete deliverables should be defined in the project
baselines. The scope baseline should be updated with the additional work, and the schedule
baseline should be updated to reflect the two-day delay. A request to update these
documents should be submitted and processed through the Perform Integrated Change
Control process.
- **D Review statement of work**
Incorrect. The statement of work is a narrative description of products, services, or results
to be delivered by a project. The statement of work does not include the breakdown of work
components. Reviewing the statement of work is not the best action for the project manager
to take in this situation.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 170
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 16 of 200
Question ID: 613637
- **A lead engineer on a construction project expresses concern about conducting the electrical and**
plumbing work in parallel. Even though performing both activities in parallel has been done
before, the engineer requests that the electrical work start after finishing the plumbing work in
order to reduce overall project risk and adhere to generally accepted best practices.
When developing the project schedule, how should the project manager define the relationship
between the electrical and plumbing work?
- **A Mandatory internal dependency**
- **B Discretionary internal dependency**
- **C Mandatory external dependency**
- **D Discretionary external dependency**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What type of dependency is established based on knowledge of best practices within a particular
application area or some unusual aspect of the project where a specific sequence is desired, even
though there may be other acceptable sequences? Is the dependency within the control of the
performing organization?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Mandatory dependencies are those that are legally or contractually required or inherent in the
nature of the work. That is not the case in this scenario. Although the engineer did 'request' that
the work be done in a certain way, which gives the impression of this being a mandatory
dependency from the project manager’s perspective, the logical relationship between the two
activities is still rooted in preferential logic. The engineer prefers the work be done in a certain
way for various reasons, but there are other acceptable sequences. And since the decision on how
to sequence the electrical and plumbing activities is within the team’s control, rather than

---

dependent on something outside the work they are doing, this is considered an internal
dependency rather than an external dependency. Therefore, of the choices given, discretionary
internal dependency is how the project manager should define the relationship between the
electrical and plumbing work.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Mandatory internal dependency**
Incorrect. Mandatory dependencies are those that are legally or contractually required or
inherent in the nature of the work. That is not the case in this scenario. A dependency
between activities is considered internal when it is inside the project team's control. While
the dependency described in the scenario fits the definition of internal dependency, part of
the answer choice is wrong. Therefore, this choice cannot be the correct answer.
- **B Discretionary internal dependency**
Correct. A dependency between activities considered discretionary where a specific
sequence is desired, but not required. In the scenario, there is no necessity - the activities
have been performed in parallel before while presumably getting the job done, but the
engineer now prefers to do them in sequence in order to reduce overall project risk and
adhere to generally accepted best practices. This is an example of a discretionary
dependency. A dependency between activities is considered internal when it is inside the
project team's control. Since the decision on how to sequence these activities comes from
within the performing organization, this is considered an internal dependency.
- **C Mandatory external dependency**
Incorrect. Mandatory dependencies are those that are legally or contractually required or
inherent in the nature of the work. That is not the case in this scenario. An external
dependency involves a relationship between project activities and non-project activities and
is typically outside the control of the project team. However, since the decision on how to
sequence the electrical and plumbing activities is within the team’s control, rather than
dependent on something outside the work they are doing, this dependency is considered
internal. Therefore, this answer choice can be eliminated.
- **D Discretionary external dependency**
Incorrect. A dependency between activities considered discretionary where a specific
sequence is desired, but not required. Although the dependency described in the question is

---

a discretionary dependency, it is not an external dependency, since the decision on how to
sequence the electrical and plumbing activities is within the team’s control.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 191-192
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 17 of 200
Question ID: 612662
You have just concluded the project kick-off meeting for a real estate development project. After
the meeting, you follow the stakeholder engagement plan by sending a survey out to all of the
meeting participants to obtain their feedback on the effectiveness of the meeting as well as any
suggestions they might have for future meetings.
After receiving the survey responses and summarizing them, what should you do next?
- **A Update the lessons learned register**
- **B Transfer any knowledge gained to the lessons learned repository**
- **C Record the information in the issue log for follow up**
- **D Submit a change request to update the stakeholder engagement plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where should the knowledge that is gained during the project be recorded?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process is being carried out by
following the stakeholder engagement plan. The lessons learned register is a project document
used to record knowledge gained during a project so that it can be used in the current project and
entered into the lessons learned repository at the end of the project. The feedback from the
meeting participants represents lessons learned, or knowledge gained, that can be used to
improve future meetings and should be documented in the lessons learned register.
Note that depending on the type of feedback received, in addition to the lessons learned register,
the issue log and the stakeholder engagement plan 'may' need to be updated as an output of the
Manage Stakeholder Engagement process. However, the lessons learned register 'should' be
updated with the feedback provided by the participants. When faced with more than one

---

potentially correct response, the PMP aspirant should select the 'best' answer to the question
asked. The answer choice that represents an activity that 'should' be performed is a better
response compared with an activity that 'might' be performed. In this case, the lesson learned
register 'should' be updated regardless of the content of the feedback. For example, if all of the
feedback is supportive of how the meeting was run, that information would only be captured in
the lessons learned register. However, if some of the stakeholders raised concerns, these concerns
may be considered issues that should be captured in the issue log. And if a resolution of these
issues requires an update to the stakeholder engagement plan, then the plan should be updated as
well (with an approved change request).

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Update the lessons learned register**
Correct. The lessons learned register is a project document used to record knowledge
gained during a project so that it can be used in the current project and entered into the
lessons learned repository at the end of the project. The feedback from the meeting
participants represents lessons learned, or knowledge gained, that can be used to improve
future meetings.
- **B Transfer any knowledge gained to the lessons learned repository**
Incorrect. The lessons learned repository is an organizational process asset that serves as a
store of historical information about lessons learned from projects. The information from
the finalized lessons learned register is transferred to the lessons learned repository at the
end of the project. Whereas, the question states that the project kick-off meeting was just
completed, which indicates that the project is either in planning or early in execution.
- **C Record the information in the issue log for follow up**
Incorrect. Any concerns raised by the stakeholders should be recorded in the issue log
where they can be tracked and monitored. However, the question does not indicate whether
or not any issues have been reported by the stakeholders in their feedback.
- **D Submit a change request to update the stakeholder engagement plan**
Incorrect. You, as the project manager, are following the stakeholder engagement plan in
this scenario. However, there is no information to suggest that the stakeholder engagement
plan needs to be updated at this point. It is possible that feedback from the participants
might lead to a change in how the stakeholders are engaged, but more information is
required to make that determination.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 529
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 18 of 200
Question ID: 613635
- **A project manager is working with his project team to develop a network diagram. During this**
process, the project team determines that the nature of work dictates that the design work must
be completed before manufacturing can start. The project manager proposes a few alternatives
but ultimately realizes that the team approach to sequence the two activities is the only way to
go.
What type of dependency does this scenario represent?
- **A Discretionary internal dependency**
- **B Mandatory external dependency**
- **C Discretionary external dependency**
- **D Mandatory internal dependency**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which type of dependency is sometimes referred to as hard logic?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question states that the project team has determined that the nature of the work requires that
design must be completed before manufacturing can start - an example of a mandatory
dependency. Mandatory dependencies are those that are legally or contractually required or
inherent in the nature of the work. And since this determination has been done by the project
team, the dependency is internal. Internal dependencies are typically inside the project team's
control. Thus, of the choices given, a mandatory internal dependency is what described by the
scenario and is, therefore, the best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Discretionary internal dependency**
Incorrect. A discretionary dependency exists between activities where a specific sequence is
desired, but not required; there may be other acceptable sequences. Internal dependencies
are typically inside the project team's control. The dependency described in the question is
determined by the team and is, therefore, internal. However, since the dependency is
required by the nature of the work, it is mandatory. Therefore, this answer choice can be
eliminated.
- **B Mandatory external dependency**
Incorrect. A mandatory dependency is one that is legally or contractually required or
inherent in the nature of the work. An external dependency involves a relationship between
project activities and non-project activities and is typically outside the control of the project
team. Since the dependency is required by the nature of the work, it is mandatory. However,
since the decision of how to sequence the activities is made by the project team, the
dependency is internal, making this choice an incorrect answer.
- **C Discretionary external dependency**
Incorrect. Discretionary dependencies exist between activities where a specific sequence is
desired, but not required. External dependencies involve a relationship between project
activities and non-project activities and are typically outside the control of the project team.
The dependency described in the question is determined by the team and is, therefore,
internal. And, since the dependency is required by the nature of the work, it is mandatory.
As such, this choice is an incorrect answer.
- **D Mandatory internal dependency**
Correct. Mandatory dependencies are those that are legally or contractually required or
inherent in the nature of the work. An internal dependency is typically inside the project
team's control. Since the dependency is required by the nature of the work, it is mandatory.
And, since the dependency is determined by the team, it is internal. Therefore, the scenario
described in the question represents a mandatory internal dependency.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 191-192

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 19 of 200
Question ID: 612133
- **A vendor is using hexavalent chrome instead of the more environmentally friendly trivalent**
chrome. You check the contract terms, and there is no stipulation requiring trivalent chrome
despite your company policy prohibiting the use of hexavalent chrome.
What was the most likely cause of this issue?
- **A The requirements documentation was either incomplete or not incorporated into the**
contract terms
- **B The quality reports failed to capture the problem**
- **C Information from the requirements traceability matrix was not included in the contract**
- **D A resource calendar was not created in the planning process**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where should you find information regarding health, safety, and environmental requirements?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Requirements documentation includes health, safety, and environmental requirements among
others. The company’s policy prohibiting the use of hexavalent chrome should have been
captured in the requirements documentation. Therefore, the requirements documentation was
either incomplete or not incorporated into the contract terms, which was the most likely cause of
the issue identified in the question.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A The requirements documentation was either incomplete or not incorporated into the**
contract terms
Correct. Requirements documentation includes health, safety, and environmental
requirements among others. The requirements documentation was either incomplete or not
incorporated into the contract terms.
- **B The quality reports failed to capture the problem**
Incorrect. The question indicates that the issue was identified while reviewing the quality
reports. Therefore, the problem was captured in the quality reports.
- **C Information from the requirements traceability matrix was not included in the contract**
Incorrect. The requirements traceability matrix is a grid that links product requirements
from their origin to the deliverables that satisfy them, but it is not a source for information
on prohibited processes.
- **D A resource calendar was not created in the planning process**
Incorrect. A resource calendar is a calendar that identifies the working days and shifts
upon which each specific resource is available. The resource calendar does not provide
information on project requirements.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 147, 148, 495

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 20 of 200
Question ID: 612092
Two qualified vendors have been identified for a project. The requesting organization is capable
of performing the work, but it was deemed less cost-effective to do so. During vendor selection,
the project manager learns that one vendor already works with a competitor and are restricted by
an exclusivity clause. The other vendor is not available during the required timeframe.
What might the project manager have done differently to avoid this situation?
- **A Included the evaluation method in the procurement documents**
- **B Obtained an independent cost estimate**
- **C Tailored the way the procurement processes were applied**
- **D Conducted a make-or-buy analysis**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

It is better to determine vendor availability before conducting procurements.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Conduct Procurements was being performed when it came to light
that there were no available vendors capable of performing the required work. Even though the
source selection criteria are not determined until project planning is performed, the basic
requirements of the project and timeline should be understood during project initiation. Because
each project is unique, the project manager should tailor the way that Project Procurement
Management processes are applied. Tailoring considerations include, among others, the
availability of contractors. Had the project manager considered the availability of contractors
before completing the procurement management plan, time and effort could have been directed
towards planning to perform the required work internally, which even if it costs more than

---

outsourcing, in the absence of available vendors, is the only viable option to completing the
project on time.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Included the evaluation method in the procurement documents**
Incorrect. It is a project management best practice to include the evaluation method in the
procurement documents, so the prospective bidders know how they will be evaluated.
However, including the evaluation method in the procurement documents would not have
changed the fact that there are no vendors available who are available to perform the
required work.
- **B Obtained an independent cost estimate**
Incorrect. The procuring organization may elect to prepare an independent estimate to
serve as a benchmark for proposed responses. However, in this scenario, there are no
available vendors capable of performing the required work. Therefore, there would not be
any proposals to evaluate.
- **C Tailored the way the procurement processes were applied**
Correct. Tailoring considerations include, among others, the availability of contractors.
Had the project manager considered the availability of contractors before completing the
procurement management plan, time and effort could have been directed towards planning
to perform the required work internally.
- **D Conducted a make-or-buy analysis**
Incorrect. The question suggests that a make-or-buy analysis was performed and it would
be more cost-effective to contract with a vendor than to perform the work with internal
resources. The availability of vendors is not typically addressed as part of the make-or-buy
analysis.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 465

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 21 of 200
Question ID: 613668
You are estimating the costs for a project where the project team will be supplemented with
independent contractors. You need to know the number of internal and external team members
assigned to the project along with the timelines for their deployment.
Where is the best place to find this information?
- **A Basis of estimates**
- **B Resource requirements**
- **C Project schedule**
- **D Cost forecasts**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where do you find the amount of time that the project team members will be active on the
project?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question indicates that the Estimate Costs process is being performed. One of the inputs to
the Estimate Costs process is the project schedule. The project schedule includes the type,
quantity, and amount of time that the team and physical resources will be active on the project.
Therefore, the project schedule is the best source of information to find a timeline for the
deployment of the team members on the project.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Basis of estimates**
Incorrect. It can be inferred from the question that the Estimate Costs process is being
carried out. The basis of estimates is an output of the Estimate Costs process and not an
input.
- **B Resource requirements**
Incorrect. Resource requirements can identify the types and quantities of resources required
for each activity in a work package. However, the resource requirements do not include the
amount of time the resources will be active on the project.
- **C Project schedule**
Correct. The project schedule includes the type, quantity, and amount of time that the team
and physical resources will be active on the project.
- **D Cost forecasts**
Incorrect. Cost forecasts are a project document that specifies a calculated estimate at
completion (EAC) or a bottom-up EAC, which is communicated to stakeholders to set
expectations on costs to be incurred by the project by the time of its completion.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 242

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 22 of 200
Question ID: 612636
You are leading an agile project to develop a computer game, which will be broken down into
four releases. After the first release, the initial online reviews are poor, and the early adopters
have provided detailed feedback about what they don't like about the game. You are concerned
about the impact of the poor reviews on future releases.
What is the best course of action?
- **A Hold a release retrospective**
- **B Terminate the project**
- **C Discuss the issue with the project sponsor**
- **D Expedite the delivery of the second release**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which option represents an action that supports continuous improvement?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Early adopters are project stakeholders. Stakeholders should be kept engaged throughout the
project life cycle. The question implies the project manager is performing the Monitor
Stakeholder Engagement process. Meetings are among the tools and techniques used in this
process. Types of meetings include status meetings, standup meetings, retrospectives, and any
other meetings as agreed upon in the stakeholder engagement plan to monitor and assess
stakeholder engagement levels. A retrospective is a scheduled review to record lessons learned.
The project manager should hold a release retrospective to analyze the feedback that has been
provided by the early adopters and take necessary actions to improve the product (the computer
game) in the upcoming releases. The knowledge gained should then be captured in the lessons
learned register and used in the current project as well as entered into the lessons learned
repository for use in future projects. Therefore, of the available options, the best course of action

---

for the project manager is to hold a retrospective to analyze the feedback that has been provided
and incorporate the knowledge gained into future releases.
Note, the fact the scenario describes an agile project does not change the correct answer. Holding
retrospectives (or lessons learned meetings) is a good practice that can be adopted by any project
regardless of the project management methodology used.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Hold a release retrospective**
Correct. A retrospective is a scheduled review to record lessons learned. The project
manager should hold a release retrospective to analyze the feedback that has been provided
by the early adopters and incorporate the knowledge gained into future releases.
- **B Terminate the project**
Incorrect. If the gaming community rejects the game, then the project may be terminated
before delivering the final release. However, terminating the project at this point in the
project is a premature action. The project manager should seek to understand the feedback
that has already been provided and use the knowledge gained to incorporate into future
releases.
- **C Discuss the issue with the project sponsor**
Incorrect. The project sponsor may or may not need to be notified of the initial customer
reviews depending on what is documented in the communications management plan.
However, discussing the matter with the project sponsor will not better align the game
design with the expectations of the gaming community.
- **D Expedite the delivery of the second release**
Incorrect. Expediting delivery of the second release without addressing feedback provided
by the early adopters of the game for the first release will unlikely make the game better. It
may lead to even worse results, a waste of the project resources, and eventually to the
project termination.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 535

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 23 of 200
Question ID: 612920
You are developing an inventory tracking software system for a retailer to scan barcodes of their
products using traditional barcode scanners. During the first sprint review, the customer
requested additional functionality to use tablets for the scanning of barcodes. The change request
has been submitted.
If the change request is approved, which of the following must be updated?
- **A The cost baseline**
- **B The schedule baseline**
- **C The scope baseline**
- **D The scope management plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The requested change represents an increase in the project scope.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scope baseline is the approved version of a scope statement, work breakdown structure
(WBS), and its associated WBS dictionary. In this scenario, the added functionality represents an
expansion of the project scope. Thus, once the change request is approved to include the
additional feature, the scope baseline must be updated to reflect the increase in project scope.
The incorrect answer choices represent baselines or a component of the project management plan
that may or may not be updated as the result of the increase in project scope. While all of the
answer choices represent items that 'might' be updated, only the scope baseline 'must' be updated
in this scenario. Therefore, of the available options, revising the scope baseline to include the
added functionality is the best answer to the question asked.

---

Note, the scenario mentions sprint review, implying the product is developed incrementally,
using agile methodologies. However, the change has been processed via a change request.
Therefore, it can be concluded that the project management approach is hybrid.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The cost baseline**
Incorrect. While it is reasonable to assume the addition in scope will require additional
resources, there is not enough information in the question to make this determination.
Therefore, the cost baseline may or may not need to be revised to account for the additional
cost. Hence, while the cost baseline 'might' need to be updated, the scope baseline 'must' be
updated.
- **B The schedule baseline**
Incorrect. While it is reasonable to assume the addition in scope will require additional
development time, there is not enough information in the question to make this
determination. Therefore, the schedule baseline may or may not need to be revised to
account for the additional cost. Hence, while the schedule baseline 'might' need to be
updated, the scope baseline 'must' be updated.
- **C The scope baseline**
Correct. In this scenario, the added functionality represents an expansion of the project
scope. Therefore, once the change request is approved to include the additional feature, the
scope baseline must be updated to reflect the increase in project scope.
- **D The scope management plan**
Incorrect. The scope management plan is the component of the project management plan
that describes how the scope will be defined, developed, monitored, controlled, and
validated. The question describes a change to the project scope rather than a change to
how the scope will be managed.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 171
