PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 72 of 200
Question ID: 612466
During project execution, the client provided updated requirements, which apparently will only
require a minor adjustment to the work breakdown structure (WBS).
What should you do first?
- **A Submit a change request to update the scope baseline**
- **B Adjust the WBS as necessary as the change is minor**
- **C Deny the request as it represents scope creep**
- **D Submit a change request to update the schedule baseline**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The work breakdown structure (WBS) is a component of the scope baseline.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that you are performing the Control Scope process, and you need to
update the work breakdown structure (WBS). The WBS is a hierarchical decomposition of the
total scope of work to be carried out by the project team to accomplish the project objectives and
create the required deliverables. The scope baseline is the approved version of a scope statement,
WBS, and its associated WBS dictionary, which can be changed only through formal change
control procedures and is used as a basis for comparison. Therefore, among the available
choices, you should first submit a change request to update the scope baseline. Note, after the
change is evaluated, additional components of the project management plan may need to be
updated. However, this option is not provided. Therefore, submitting a change request to update
the scope baseline is the best response.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Submit a change request to update the scope baseline**
Correct. The WBS is a component of the scope baseline. An approved change request is
required to update any of the project baselines including their components.
- **B Adjust the WBS as necessary as the change is minor**
Incorrect. The WBS is a component of the scope baseline. Any change to a project baseline
requires an approved change request of how small the request apparently is. Other project
constraints might be affected as the result of the change. Therefore, adjusting the WBS
without an approved change will likely go against the organization's change control
process established for the project.
- **C Deny the request as it represents scope creep**
Incorrect. Scope creep is the uncontrolled expansion of product or project scope without
adjustments to time, cost, and resources. Implementing the changes to the WBS might
represent scope creep, but not if a change request is submitted and approved first.
Additionally, there would be no reason to deny the change without first submitting a change
request where the change can be analyzed against all project constraints to render a
decision. The change request may then be approved, denied, or deferred.
- **D Submit a change request to update the schedule baseline**
Incorrect. The question states that a request has been made to modify the WBS, which is a
component of the scope baseline, not the schedule baseline. It is possible that after
analyzing the change request as part of the Perform Integrated Change Control Process,
that the schedule baseline may be affected, but that is not known based on the information
presented by the question. It is also possible that the change to the WBS can be
accommodated without adjusting the schedule baseline.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 170, 161
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 73 of 200
Question ID: 612668
- **A project manager is leading a large project to develop a new model of smartphone. Early in**
project execution, to foster the stakeholder involvement, the project manager holds a meeting as
specified in the stakeholder engagement plan.
What type of meeting does the project manager likely hold?
- **A A project retrospective to finalize lessons learned register**
- **B A workshop to develop the team charter**
- **C A project kick-off meeting to establish roles and responsibilities of stakeholders**
- **D A meeting to create a comprehensive list of stakeholders**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What type of meeting might be held during the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The stakeholder engagement plan is a component of the project management plan that identifies
the strategies and actions required to promote the productive involvement of stakeholders in
project decision making and execution. The stakeholder engagement plan is created as an output
of the Plan Stakeholder Engagement process and followed during the Manage Stakeholder
Engagement process. Thus, the question is asking which type of meeting might be held during
the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process. A kick-off meeting is one of the types of meetings
that may be held in support of the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process to foster the
appropriate level of stakeholder involvement in the project. The incorrect answer choices
represent meetings that are exclusive to other project management processes and would not be
held as part of the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process. Therefore, of the available choices,
the project manager is most likely holding a project kick-off meeting.

---

Note, the scenario describes a large project in its early execution stage. In large projects, the
kick-off meeting takes place with processes in the Executing Process Group, thus additionally
supporting the correct answer.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A A project retrospective to finalize lessons learned register**
Incorrect. A project retrospective is held at the end of a project as part of the Close Project
or Phase process, and not during the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process, as implied
by the question.
- **B A workshop to develop the team charter**
Incorrect. The team charter is developed as an output of the Plan Resource Management
process, whereas the question describes the meeting as supporting the Manage Stakeholder
Engagement process. Additionally, the team charter is focused on the project team, while
the question is concerned with the stakeholder engagement.
- **C A project kick-off meeting to establish roles and responsibilities of stakeholders**
Correct. The question implies that the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process is being
performed. A kick-off meeting is one of the types of meetings that may be held in support of
that process.
- **D A meeting to create a comprehensive list of stakeholders**
Incorrect. This answer choice describes the creation of the stakeholder register. The
stakeholder register is created as an output of the Identify Stakeholders process during
project initiation, while the scenario describes a project in execution.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 528, 86

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 74 of 200
Question ID: 612230
You are managing a manufacturing process improvement project. A key stakeholder suggests a
correction to the procedure being used to identify defects in the product. You agree that the
modified procedure will better help identify defects. You submit a change request to modify the
procedure and have the change approved.
When implementing the change request, you should document the updated procedure in all of the
following places, except?
- **A Lessons learned register**
- **B Quality management plan**
- **C Organizational process assets**
- **D Stakeholder register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What would help ensure that the updated procedure will be used for future defects identification?
Note, the question is looking for an exception.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Approved change requests are implemented in the Direct and Manage Project Work process,
which is part of the Executing Process Group. Updates to the quality management plan (a
component of the project management plan), organizational process assets, and lessons learned
register are among the outputs of this process. Updating these project artifacts would help ensure
that the improved procedure will be used for defects identification in future project work.
However, the question is looking for an exception. The stakeholder register does not contain
information about procedures used on the project, and therefore should not be updated. The fact
that the improved procedure has been suggested by a stakeholder does not affect any information

---

about the stakeholder themselves making the update of the stakeholder register unnecessary.
Hence, of the available choices, the stakeholder register is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Lessons learned register**
Incorrect. A lessons learned register is a project document that records knowledge gained
throughout the project. Adding the improved procedure for identifying defects to the lessons
learned register would help ensure the new procedure will be used for future defect
identification. Therefore updates to the lessons learned register is not an exception, making
this choice an incorrect answer.
- **B Quality management plan**
Incorrect. The quality management plan describes how applicable policies and procedures
will be implemented to achieve quality objectives, including quality control and quality
management activities. Procedures for defects identification will likely be included in the
quality management plan making it not an exception. Therefore, this answer choice can be
eliminated.
- **C Organizational process assets**
Incorrect. Organizational process assets (OPAs) include policies, procedures, and
guidelines for managing quality and eliminating defects. Since OPAs are internal to the
organization, the project team members can update them and add to the OPAs as necessary
throughout the project. Updates to the OPAs exclude them from the list of exceptions,
making this choice not the best answer to the question asked.
- **D Stakeholder register**
Correct. The stakeholder register is a project document that captures information about
project stakeholders and their identification, assessment, and classification. It is the only
document of the choices shown that would not be updated when implementing the change
request to use the improved procedure for identifying defects, even though the source of the
change request was a stakeholder.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 95-97, 39

---

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 75 of 200
Question ID: 612465
At the beginning of your project, you were authorized to offer incentives to the designers to work
in your company's office building for the duration of the project. You secured a temporary
workspace to accommodate the entire project design team in a common area. This strategy
allows them to work in proximity to one another to enhance their ability to perform as a unified
design team.
What tool or technique did you use in this scenario?
- **A Virtual teams**
- **B Colocation**
- **C Forming**
- **D Strategic placement**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Proximity is a key benefit of this technique used in the Develop Team process.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Colocation is one of the tools and techniques used in the Develop Team process. Colocation
involves placing many or all of the most active project team members in the same physical
location to enhance their ability to perform as a team. Keeping the team members in the same
physical location helps create an effective, productive team.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Virtual teams**
Incorrect. This scenario describes a team that will be working in the same physical
location; virtual teams spend little or no time meeting face-to-face.
- **B Colocation**
Correct. The question describes an organizational strategy that places a project team in the
same physical location to improve communication, working relationships, and project
productivity.
- **C Forming**
Incorrect. Forming is a phase in the Tuckman ladder team development theory, not a tool
or a technique of the Develop Team process described in the scenario.
- **D Strategic placement**
Incorrect. 'Strategic placement' is a fake technique made up for this question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 340

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 76 of 200
Question ID: 626034
At a meeting during project initiation, the project manager and the project sponsor present the
project charter to the key project stakeholders. Decisions should be made and actions assigned to
some of the stakeholders. However, not all meeting participants completely agree with the
project vision and objectives.
What should the project manager do to gain the support of the stakeholders for the decisions and
actions made during the meeting?
- **A Request the project sponsor force the decisions and actions on the stakeholders**
- **B Try to reach a consensus among the stakeholders**
- **C Do nothing; it is not important to have the support of the stakeholders during project**
initiation
- **D Dismiss the meeting participants and terminate the project**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project manager should use their soft skills.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

It is unlikely that all project stakeholders will always be 100% in agreement about everything on
the project. Often, the stakeholders will have competing goals. The project manager should use
their soft skills, such as interpersonal skills and the ability to manage people, to balance the
conflicting and competing goals of the project stakeholders in order to achieve consensus.
Consensus does not require that everybody is in complete agreement. While there could be a
disagreement with some of the project goals, the stakeholders commit to and support the project
decisions and actions. Therefore, to foster the stakeholders' commitment and increase the chance

---

of project success, the project manager should try to reach consensus among the project
stakeholders.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Request the project sponsor force the decisions and actions on the stakeholders**
Incorrect. Forcing is the least desirable approach when there is a difference in opinions.
Forcing is unlikely to lead to project stakeholder support for the decisions and actions
reached during the meeting.
- **B Try to reach a consensus among the stakeholders**
Correct. When meeting participants are not 100% in agreement, project managers should
use their soft skills to reach consensus among the attendees and gain their commitment and
support to the meeting's decisions and actions.
- **C Do nothing; it is not important to have the support of the stakeholders during project**
initiation
Incorrect. It is important to have the support of the stakeholders throughout the project life
cycle. Without their support, the chance of project success is diminished.
- **D Dismiss the meeting participants and terminate the project**
Incorrect. This action is too extreme. There is not enough information in the question to
assume the disagreements among the stakeholders are so severe that dismissing the meeting
participants and terminating the project is the only reasonable action to be taken.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 53-54

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 77 of 200
Question ID: 626014
All project deliverables are completed and approved by the customer. The sponsor congratulates
the project manager for successful execution.
What should the project manager do next?
- **A Nothing. The project is complete.**
- **B Transfer the product to the customer**
- **C Take the team to a celebration party**
- **D Perform the procurement audit**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Is your project formally complete when all planned work is done, and the customer is satisfied?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question does not say that the project is complete. Rather, it says: "All planned work on your
project has been completed." The project is formally complete only when all actions and
activities listed in the Close Project or Phase process are completed. The closing actions and
activities include: obtaining final acceptance of the project deliverables, obtaining financial,
legal, and administrative closure, communicating the final project report to the stakeholders,
collating lessons learned that were documented throughout the project, archiving project
documents, and transferring the ownership of the project deliverables to the customer or the
assigned stakeholders in accordance with the project management plan.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Nothing. The project is complete.**
Incorrect. Just because all the planned work on the project has been completed, and the
customer has approved the deliverables does not mean the project is complete. The project
is complete only when all closing activities are completed.
- **B Transfer the product to the customer**
Correct. The project is complete only when all closing activities are completed. One of the
activities that should be performed as part of the Close Project or Phase process is a
transition of the ownership of deliverables to the customer or the assigned stakeholders in
accordance with the project management plan to facilitate the formal project closure.
- **C Take the team to a celebration party**
Incorrect. While there is nothing wrong with taking the project team to a celebration party
after all planned work is done, there is another answer choice which better addresses the
question asked.
- **D Perform the procurement audit**
Incorrect. There is no information in the question to determine if the project involved any
procurements.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 123

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 78 of 200
Question ID: 612414
You are planning a project to develop a new video game. The project will consist of three
releases, five iterations per release. The first release will provide the must-have features required
for a minimum viable product with additional features added after each subsequent release. The
customer wants to know which features will be available at the end of each iteration.
What is the best tool or technique to use in this situation?
- **A Project schedule**
- **B Milestone list**
- **C Agile release planning**
- **D Critical path method**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What technique provides a high-level summary timeline of the release schedule and defines
which features will be available at the end of each iteration?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Agile release planning provides a high-level summary timeline of the release schedule based on
the product roadmap and the product vision for the product's evolution. Since features represent
value to the customer, the timeline provides a more easily understood project schedule as it
defines which features will be available at the end of each iteration, which is precisely the depth
of information the customer is looking for.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Project schedule**
Incorrect. The project schedule is an output of a schedule model that presents linked
activities with planned dates, durations, milestones, and resources. The project schedule is
not likely to list the specific features that will be available at the end of each release. Also,
the project schedule is not a tool or technique.
- **B Milestone list**
Incorrect. A milestone is a significant point or event in a project. A milestone list identifies
all project milestones and indicates whether a milestone is mandatory or optional. The
milestone list may have information on release dates but not specific information on which
features will be available at the end of each iteration. Additionally, the milestone list is not
a tool or technique.
- **C Agile release planning**
Correct. Agile release planning provides a high-level summary timeline of the release
schedule and defines which features will be available at the end of each iteration.
- **D Critical path method**
Incorrect. The critical path method is a method used to estimate the minimum project
duration and determine the amount of scheduling flexibility on the logical network paths
within the schedule model. However, the critical path method does not provide insight into
the features that will be associated with each iteration.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 216

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 79 of 200
Question ID: 612126
- **A senior executive shares her opinion with the project manager that the production is too**
labor-intensive, such that profit margins are shrinking. The company must reduce labor costs
significantly through automation if it is to survive.
What is the project manager’s best course of action in this situation?
- **A Start developing a business case**
- **B Do nothing until a project charter has been approved**
- **C Suggest that the senior executive initiate a project**
- **D Ask to be designated as the project sponsor and begin project initiation**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How is an organization transformed from the current state to a desired future state?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

In this scenario, a production line needs to be updated to reduce labor costs for the long-term
viability of the company. Thus, the current production process must be transformed. Projects
drive change in organizations. From a business perspective, a project is aimed at moving an
organization from one state to another state to achieve a specific objective. Before the project
begins, the organization is commonly referred to as being in the current state. The desired result
of the change driven by the project is described as the future state.
In this case, a project should be initiated to transform the organization from the current state to
the desired future state. Although a project manager cannot initiate a project, a project manager
can make suggestions as to how the organizational objectives can be accomplished. Therefore, of

---

the available choices, suggesting that the senior executive initiate a project is the best course of
action in this situation.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Start developing a business case**
Incorrect. A business case is a documented economic feasibility study used to establish the
validity of the benefits of a selected component lacking sufficient definition and that is used
as a basis for the authorization of further project management activities. The project
sponsor is generally accountable for the development and maintenance of the project
business case and not the project manager.
- **B Do nothing until a project charter has been approved**
Incorrect. A project manager may be involved in a project prior to the approval of the
project charter. A project manager may even assist with the creation of the project charter.
Additionally, a project manager may make recommendations to senior executives and/or a
project sponsor. In this situation, doing nothing when a problem or opportunity arises is not
appropriate
- **C Suggest that the senior executive initiate a project**
Correct. Projects drive change in organizations. From a business perspective, a project is
aimed at moving an organization from one state to another state to achieve a specific
objective.
- **D Ask to be designated as the project sponsor and begin project initiation**
Incorrect. A project sponsor is external to the project. Additionally, the project sponsor
should be at a level to secure funding and resources for the project. A project manager is
internal to the project and is not likely to be in a position to secure funding and resources
for a project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 6
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 80 of 200
Question ID: 612233
You are managing a state-of-the-art technology design project. You have just implemented an
approved change request that required crashing with new resources.
This requires all of the following to be updated except:
- **A Project scope**
- **B Project schedule**
- **C Project costs**
- **D Risk register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What project constraints are affected by hiring additional resources? Remember, the question is
looking for an exception.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Crashing is a schedule compression technique that involves adding resources to project schedule
activities so that they can divide up the work and therefore get it done in less time.
Implementation of this technique usually requires additional costs to pay for the added resources
(the new project team members in this case). Typically, the new team members need to be
on-boarded, and the work among them should be divided up and coordinated. Frequently, this
increases the risk of errors and the need for rework. However, the resulting work product, or the
deliverables, that the team should complete remains unchanged. Therefore, the project scope is
unlikely to change when crashing is applied. Since the question is looking for an exception,
project scope is the best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Project scope**
Correct. The point of crashing is to accelerate the schedule without reducing the project
scope. The change proposed in this scenario would not incur adjustment to scope. So the
scope baseline is the exception this question seeks and is, therefore, the correct answer.
- **B Project schedule**
Incorrect. Crashing brings the project back on schedule by shortening the activities on the
critical path. With crashing, you are assigning additional resources or overtime to project
schedule activities. You update the schedule to reflect the new resources and the tasks to
which they are assigned. Since the project schedule will require adjustments, it is not the
exception, making this choice an incorrect answer.
- **C Project costs**
Incorrect. Crashing usually incurs additional labor costs to pay for more resources or
overtime on project schedule activities. It may be possible to use contingency reserves to
cover the additional costs and still stay within the cost baseline, but you will need to
account for the use of the reserves. Since the cost accounting will require adjustments,
project costs are not the exception, and therefore this choice can be eliminated.
- **D Risk register**
Incorrect. Crashing adds risks due to increased coordination and increased chance of
errors or rework. In the case of approving overtime, the assigned resources have an
increased potential for burnout. Therefore, the risk register will need to be updated, which
excludes it from the list of exceptions and makes this choice an incorrect answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 215
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 81 of 200
Question ID: 612232
As a new project manager, you have kept your project on track by relying on control and
focusing on the bottom line. Although the project team is doing what has been asked of them,
they feel that they are being micromanaged and lack the autonomy to make independent
decisions for the betterment of the project.
How might you improve the performance of the team?
- **A Become a more inspirational leader by improving your management skills**
- **B Ask the project team to focus more on systems and structure**
- **C Develop leadership skills to inspire trust and focus more on the horizon**
- **D Focus your attention more on operational issues and problem-solving**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Management relies on control and focuses on the bottom line.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question describes a situation where you, as the project manager, are relying exclusively on
management to keep the project on track. The consequence of this leadership style is that the
project team lacks the autonomy to perform optimally. Developing leadership skills and focusing
more on the horizon will inspire trust and improve the performance of the team. All the incorrect
answer choices are related to emphasizing management over leadership, which will be
counterproductive in this situation. Therefore, of the available options, developing leadership
skills to inspire trust and focusing more on the horizon is the best approach to improve team
performance.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Become a more inspirational leader by improving your management skills**
Incorrect. The question describes a situation where you, as a project manager, are
emphasizing management over leadership. You need to improve your leadership skills
rather than management skills.
- **B Ask the project team to focus more on systems and structure**
Incorrect. A focus on systems and structure is an example of management over leadership.
To inspire trust, you, as the project manager, should emphasize leadership, which should
provide a more productive environment for the project team.
- **C Develop leadership skills to inspire trust and focus more on the horizon**
Correct. Developing leadership skills and focusing more on the horizon inspires trust and
helps to enhance the performance of the team.
- **D Focus your attention more on operational issues and problem-solving**
Incorrect. The problem described by the question is that you, as the project manager, are
relying exclusively on management rather than leadership to keep the project on track.
Focusing on operational issues and problem-solving is an example of management over
leadership.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 64

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 82 of 200
Question ID: 613286
You are managing a process improvement project and have interviewed different stakeholders
over the past few weeks to understand the various suppliers, products supplied, manufacturing
steps, and inputs and outputs. You are now in a very good position to start analyzing the
processes.
What should you do next?
- **A Determine the cost of conformance**
- **B Determine the cost of non-conformance**
- **C Use control charts to analyze the processes**
- **D Create a SIPOC model**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

After the interviews have provided a large quantity of raw information, you next need to
organize it visually to help analyze the various suppliers and processes.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

According to the scenario provided, you are performing the Plan Quality Management process.
You have obtained enough information regarding your customer's processes to enable you to start
analyzing them, and the next step is to visually document the processes using a data
representation tool, such as a flowchart. The SIPOC (suppliers, inputs, processes, outputs,
customers) model is an example of a flowchart that is specifically designed for
analyzing suppliers and process interactions in a manufacturing environment and, of the choices
provided, is the best tool to use.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Determine the cost of conformance**
Incorrect. The cost of conformance is money spent during the project to avoid failure.
Determining the cost of conformance provides the prevention component of the cost of
quality, but this does not help with the analysis of specific processes or their interactions.
- **B Determine the cost of non-conformance**
Incorrect. The cost of non-conformance is money spent during and after the project because
of failures. Determining the cost of non-conformance provides the internal and external
failure components of the cost of quality but does not help to analyze specific processes or
their interactions.
- **C Use control charts to analyze the processes**
Incorrect. Control charts are used to determine whether or not a process is stable using
statistical plotting. However, they are not used for general process analysis.
- **D Create a SIPOC model**
Correct. SIPOC models are a type of flowchart designed to help visualize the interactions
between suppliers, inputs, processes, outputs, and customers in a coherent value chain.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 284-285

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 83 of 200
Question ID: 612259
- **A project manager invited several vendors to a pre-bid conference. After a private conversation**
with one of the vendors who had an inquiry about a new mandatory government requirement, the
project manager sent an email to the vendor to address the question. The project manager realizes
that the requirement should have been included in the project scope baseline and the statement of
work (SOW).
What should the project manager do in this situation?
- **A No further action is needed as the vendor's question have been addressed**
- **B Update the statement of work and the scope baseline, and communicate the changes to all**
vendors
- **C Update the statement of work and the scope baseline, and hold another pre-bid conference**
- **D Update the SOW, submit a change request to update the scope baseline, and communicate**
the changes to all vendors
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Consider that the requirement needs to be added to a project baseline and that the project
manager needs to be fair to all vendors.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

According to the scenario, the project manager is performing the Conduct Procurements process.
- **A bidder conference (also called a contractor conference, vendor conference, and a pre-bid**
conference) is one of the tools and techniques used as part of this process. The project manager
should be fair to all vendors and abide by the value of fairness in the PMI Code of Ethics and
Professional Conduct. Project managers should constantly re-examine their impartiality and
objectivity, taking corrective action as needed. The project manager, in this scenario, should
provide equal access to information to those who are authorized to have that information. The

---

missed requirement should also be added to the project scope baseline, which requires the
Perform Integrated Change Control process to be carried out, including an approved change
request.
Note, a procurement SOW can be revised as required as it moves through the procurement
process until incorporated into a signed agreement. After that, if the SOW requires an update, an
approved changed request is needed to modify it as it is part of the agreement. While this point is
not covered by the correct answer choice, updating the SOW, submitting a change request to
update the scope baseline, and communicating the changes to all vendors is still the best answer
of those provided.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A No further action is needed as the vendor's question have been addressed**
Incorrect. The project manager’s response may give that vendor an unfair advantage in
bidding.
- **B Update the statement of work and the scope baseline, and communicate the changes to all**
vendors
Incorrect. The procurement statement of work is the description of the procurement item
based on the scope baseline and should indeed be updated. The changes should be
communicated to the vendors. The scope baseline is part of the project management plan
and is, therefore a controlled document. This answer is incorrect since it skips the change
control procedure.
- **C Update the statement of work and the scope baseline, and hold another pre-bid conference**
Incorrect. Another pre-bid conference is one way to communicate clearly to all vendors in
fairness for the procurement process. However, since the scope baseline is part of the
project management plan, it is a controlled document which cannot be updated without an
approved change request. This choice skips the Perform Integrated Change Control
process.
- **D Update the SOW, submit a change request to update the scope baseline, and communicate**
the changes to all vendors
Correct. Changes to the baseline must undergo the Perform Integrated Change Control
process. A change to the statement of work should be clearly communicated to all vendors.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 486-491, 478, 496. See also PMI Code of
Ethics and Professional Conduct, Fairness.

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 84 of 200
Question ID: 612562
You are leading a project with a critical time constraint and cannot afford any project delays. An
argument between two project team members turns into a shouting match. The team members
draw you into their argument on selecting a report format.
What is your best course of action?
- **A Tell the team members to figure it out for themselves**
- **B Look for an approach that would completely satisfy both team members**
- **C Request the team members to go back to work to avoid any further delays**
- **D Select the report format that you think is best and make the decision**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Your choice of the most appropriate conflict resolution method can be influenced by factors
present at the time of the conflict.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Your success in managing a project and your team often depends on your ability to resolve
conflict appropriately and promptly. You should choose the most appropriate conflict resolution
method based on factors such as the importance and the intensity of the conflict and timelines.
According to the scenario, you need to address the dispute quickly so that the team members can
return to work without further delay. The quickest way to resolve the conflict in this situation,
and, therefore, your best course of action, is to use the force/direct method by selecting an
approach that you think is the best and make the decision. Note, the collaborative or
problem-solving approach, which incorporates multiple viewpoints and insights from different
perspectives, is ideal to resolve conflicts. However, such an approach is not always possible.

---

Project managers should use their interpersonal and team skills and situational judgment to
determine how best to handle a conflict.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Tell the team members to figure it out for themselves**
Incorrect. Telling the team members to figure it out for themselves is an example of the
withdraw/avoid technique where you retreat from the situation allowing it to be fixed later
or by others. This method would take time that you cannot afford. Therefore, this approach
is not the best way to resolve the conflict.
- **B Look for an approach that would completely satisfy both team members**
Incorrect. Looking for a resolution to the conflict that would completely satisfy both parties
is an example of the collaborate/ problem-solving technique, which leads to a win-win
solution. A win-win solution would take time and is not realistic given your short timeline
and the intensity of the conflict.
- **C Request the team members to go back to work to avoid any further delays**
Incorrect. Since the project has a critical time constraint and cannot afford any delays,
requesting the team members to go back to work may be a plausible option. However, this
approach may harm the project manager's reputation and is not consistent with the best
practices of being a servant leader for the project team.
- **D Select the report format that you think is best and make the decision**
Correct. Pushing one team member's viewpoint at the expense of another's is an example of
the force/direct technique of conflict resolution. Although this method often results in a
win-lose situation, this choice is best so you can quickly stop the intense argument and
enable the team members to return to work without further delay.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 348-349
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 85 of 200
Question ID: 613669
- **A project manager needs to use a unique, new technology on a project, so there are numerous**
unknowns for the project, which will affect project planning. The project manager is currently
estimating the costs for the project and needs to be as accurate and detailed as possible.
What tool or technique is best for the project manager to use in this situation?
- **A Bottom-up estimating**
- **B Parametric estimating**
- **C Analogous estimating**
- **D Estimate Activity Durations**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which estimating technique is best for a project with a new and unique product?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the Estimate Costs process is underway. Bottom-up, analogous, and
parametric are all estimating techniques that may be used during the Estimate Costs process.
Both analogous and parametric estimating rely on historical data which is not available for a
project with a product that is new and unique as described in the question. Bottom-up estimating
is a method of estimating project cost by aggregating the estimates of the lower-level
components of the work breakdown structure (WBS). Therefore, without historical data, the
bottom-up estimating technique is the best choice.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Bottom-up estimating**
Correct. Bottom-up estimating is a method of estimating project cost by aggregating the
estimates of the lower-level components of the work breakdown structure (WBS). The
question describes a product which is new and unique. Therefore, historical data would not
be available in this situation, making bottom-up estimating the best choice.
- **B Parametric estimating**
Incorrect. Parametric estimating is an estimating technique in which an algorithm is used
to calculate the cost based on historical data and project parameters. Since historical data
does not exist for a product which is new and unique, parametric estimating is not the best
choice.
- **C Analogous estimating**
Incorrect. Analogous estimating is a technique for estimating the cost of an activity or a
project using historical data from a similar activity or project. The question states that the
technology for the product is unique with the implication being that historical data from a
similar project does not exist. Since analogous estimating relies on historical data, this
would not be the best choice in this circumstance.
- **D Estimate Activity Durations**
Incorrect. Estimate Activity Durations is a project management process and not a tool or
technique.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 244

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 86 of 200
Question ID: 613347
- **A new product development project went exceptionally well, finishing ahead of schedule and**
under budget. The project manager is just starting project closure and wants to identify the
factors that led to the project's success so that the results can be replicated for future projects.
What is the best course of action for the project manager?
- **A Perform a regression analysis**
- **B Review the risk register**
- **C Measure stakeholder satisfaction**
- **D Study the project's final report**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which data analysis tool might be beneficial in this situation?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

It is most likely that a combination of factors was responsible for the remarkable success of the
project. The project manager must try to understand if and how multiple actions contributed to
the project’s overall success. Regression analysis is an analytical technique where a series of
input variables are examined in relation to their corresponding output results in order to develop
a mathematical or statistical relationship. For project closure, regression analysis is a technique
that analyzes the interrelationships between different project variables that contributed to the
project outcomes, which can be used to improve performance on future projects. Therefore,
among the available options, performing a regression analysis is the best course of action.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Perform a regression analysis**
Correct. For project closure, regression analysis is a technique that analyzes the
interrelationships between different project variables that contributed to the project
outcomes, which can be used to improve performance on future projects.
- **B Review the risk register**
Incorrect. A risk register is a repository where outputs of the risk management processes
are recorded. While the risk register specifies risks and their implemented responses, this
information alone would not help the project manager identify the factors that led to the
project's success so that the results can be replicated for future projects.
- **C Measure stakeholder satisfaction**
Incorrect. Measuring stakeholder satisfaction is an activity associated with the Close
Project or Phase process described in the scenario. However, as its name implies, this
activity is not intended to determine the factors that contributed to the project's success and
is, therefore, not the best answer to the question asked.
- **D Study the project's final report**
Incorrect. The project's final report may have valuable information regarding the project's
success. However, the question states that the project manager is just starting project
closure, and the final report is an output of this process. Hence, in this scenario, the final
report has yet to be developed.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 126

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 87 of 200
Question ID: 612334
- **A project manager has yet to be assigned to a project. The project sponsor asked a group from**
the project management office (PMO) to get together and discuss the high-level risks of the
project and the overall project risk for inclusion in the project charter. After the meeting, the
sponsor receives feedback that two of the participants dominated the meeting and others did not
have the opportunity to provide their insights.
How might this situation have been avoided?
- **A Delaying project initiation until a project manager was named**
- **B Ensuring that someone in the group was skilled in meeting management**
- **C Designating someone with strong conflict management skills to lead the meeting**
- **D Assigning a skilled facilitator to lead the meeting**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which interpersonal and team skill associated with the Develop Project Charter process ensures
that there is effective participation and that all contributions are considered?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the Develop Project Charter is being performed by the project
sponsor. Interpersonal and team skills which may support this process include conflict
management, facilitation, and meeting management; all of which are offered as answer choices.
The question describes a situation where not all of the participants of the group event had an
opportunity to provide their insights. Facilitation is the ability to effectively guide a group event
to a successful decision, solution, or conclusion. A facilitator ensures that there is effective
participation, that participants achieve a mutual understanding, and that all contributions are

---

considered. Therefore, of the available options, assigning a skilled facilitator to lead the meeting
is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Delaying project initiation until a project manager was named**
Incorrect. A project manager may or may not be assigned during project initiation. The
project charter is the document that names the project manager and provides the project
manager with the authority to apply organizational resources to the project. While it may
be best to have the project manager assist with the development of the project charter, in
some cases, there is no reason to delay the project if the project sponsor is willing to
oversee the completion of the charter.
- **B Ensuring that someone in the group was skilled in meeting management**
Incorrect. Effective meeting management skills may or may not have beneficial in this
situation. Meeting management includes preparing the agenda, ensuring that the
appropriate stakeholders are invited, and preparing and sending the follow-up minutes and
actions. Meeting management addresses the meeting logistics rather than how skillfully the
meeting is led.
- **C Designating someone with strong conflict management skills to lead the meeting**
Incorrect. Conflict management can be a valuable skill in the development of the project
charter to bring stakeholders into alignment on the elements of the charter. However, the
question describes a situation where some of the participants were not offered an
opportunity to provide their insights, rather than an issue of conflict between the
stakeholders.
- **D Assigning a skilled facilitator to lead the meeting**
Correct. A facilitator ensures that there is effective participation, that participants achieve
a mutual understanding, and that all contributions are considered. Having a skilled
facilitator to lead the meeting would likely have helped the less vocal meeting participants
to provide their insights and avoid the situation described in the scenario.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 80

---

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 88 of 200
Question ID: 612218
You are leading a software development project that is running behind schedule. The project
team was so inspired and motivated by your vision for the project, a truly exceptional product is
being developed, but numerous unaddressed operational issues have delayed the project.
What might you have done differently to have kept the project on schedule?
- **A Relied exclusively on management skills in handling the project**
- **B Developed better leadership skills**
- **C Struck the right balance between management and leadership**
- **D Selected a more detail-oriented project team**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

You, as the project manager, were highly inspirational and motivational to the project team but
lacked in administrating operational aspects of the project.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question implies that you, as the project manager, have overemphasized leadership at the
expense of management. Although you were highly effective at inspiring and motivating the
project team to create a truly exceptional product, operational aspects of the project have not
been addressed causing the project delays. Project managers need to employ both leadership and
management in order to be successful. A project manager must strike the right balance between
management and leadership to be successful. Had you focused more on management and the
operational aspects of the project, you may have been able to avoid the delays and kept the
project on schedule.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Relied exclusively on management skills in handling the project**
Incorrect. A successful project manager must find the right balance between management
and leadership. Relying exclusively on one or the other is not likely to provide optimal
performance.
- **B Developed better leadership skills**
Incorrect. The question suggests you, and the project manager, have demonstrated effective
leadership skills by inspiring and motivating the project team. However, your management
skills are lacking as demonstrated by numerous unaddressed operational issues.
- **C Struck the right balance between management and leadership**
Correct. The question implies that you, as the project manager, have overemphasized
leadership at the expense of management. A project manager must strike the right balance
between management and leadership to be successful.
- **D Selected a more detail-oriented project team**
Incorrect. The question implies that the schedule issues are more likely the result of a lack
of management skills rather than how detail-oriented the team members are.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 64

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 89 of 200
Question ID: 651309
The project cost baseline was revised and updated.
What was the most likely reason for this revision?
- **A Implementation of a planned risk response**
- **B An authorized change**
- **C A change in team composition**
- **D The CPI was outside of control limits**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

When does a project baseline ever change?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The project cost baseline is the approved version of the time-phased project budget, excluding
any management reserves, which can be changed only through formal change control
procedures. It is used as a basis for comparison to actual results. If the baseline is constantly
readjusted, then it would be difficult to compare plans to actual results. Hence a revision to the
cost baseline would most likely be due to an authorized change.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Implementation of a planned risk response**

---

Incorrect. Risk responses are typically accounted for by contingency reserves that have
been put aside during project planning. Contingency reserves, along with the work package
cost estimates, are part of the cost baseline. When a planned risk response is implemented,
costs associated with its implementation are covered by the contingency reserves.
Therefore, no change to the cost baseline is required.
- **B An authorized change**
Correct. The cost baseline is the approved version of the project budget. Only authorized
changes that have gone through the formal change control procedures regulated by your
project can alter and change your cost baseline.
- **C A change in team composition**
Incorrect. A change in team composition may or may not result in an update to the cost
baseline. For example, an acquisition of additional team members may require additional
funds which should be accounted for in the cost baseline. However, if one team member is
replaced by another one without any impact on the costs, the cost baseline would remain
unchanged. Therefore, of the choices provided, a change in team composition is not the
most likely reason for the update to the cost baseline.
- **D The CPI was outside of control limits**
Incorrect. The cost performance index going outside the control limits may be a cause as to
why the cost baseline was revised and updated, but it is not necessarily a one to one
correlation. Other reasons may have prompted the change.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 254, 269
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 90 of 200
Question ID: 651318
Your project is nearing completion. Deadlines are extremely tight. Product testing has been
moved up a day to align with resource constraints. Many minor issues are detected by testing;
errors which could pose serious delays.
What is your best action?
- **A Speed up testing to meet the completion date and hand off to the quality team**
- **B Halt further testing until the identified issues are fully resolved**
- **C Complete a Pareto chart and triage the issues with the project team**
- **D Inform the customer that the product has issues and assure that everything is to be**
delivered on time as promised
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Is there a tool to help organize the issues?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Product testing is typically performed as part of the Control Quality process. Testing is an
organized and constructed investigation conducted to provide objective information about the
quality of the product or service under test in accordance with the project requirements. The
primary goal of product testing is to uncover defects. Once the defects are found, a Pareto chart
can present the project team with the frequency of the defects’ appearance per their source and
help the team prioritize the sources that cause the greatest number of defects. Addressing these
sources would likely reduce the risk of having further delays described in the scenario.
While the topic of this question is only briefly covered in the PMBOK® Guide, the Project
Management Professional (PMP)® Examination Content Outline, June 2015, specifies

---

knowledge and skills with which PMP aspirants are expected to be familiar. Various quality
control tools and techniques, such as Pareto charts, are among these topics.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Speed up testing to meet the completion date and hand off to the quality team**
Incorrect. More and faster product testing may assist in uncovering more issues, however, it
does not eliminate the issues or fix those discovered.
- **B Halt further testing until the identified issues are fully resolved**
Incorrect. Testing may not need to cease. Testing may even help with resolution.
- **C Complete a Pareto chart and triage the issues with the project team**
Correct. A Pareto chart is a special form of vertical bar chart that can be used to identify
the vital few sources that are responsible for causing most of the problem’s effects.
Understanding the most frequent issues – especially since the issues have been deemed as
‘minor issues’ – allows the project team to better allocate their energy and resources.
- **D Inform the customer that the product has issues and assure that everything is to be**
delivered on time as promised
Incorrect. There is no delay at this point as well as no assurance that the project and its
product are to meet promised dates with the information given in the question. Making false
and unbacked claims to your customer is not advised and may violate values outlined in the
PMI Code of Ethics and Professional Conduct.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 304; see
also https://www.pmi.org/learning/library/defects-spacecraft-electronics-2022
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 91 of 200
Question ID: 613803
You are looking for the information that includes the analysis of the probability of successfully
completing the project. This analysis takes into account the legal, economic, technological,
scheduling, and other factors when calculated.
Which of the following would provide the information you seek?
- **A Bid documents**
- **B Feasibility study**
- **C Plausibility study**
- **D Needs assessment**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

This item would provide validity to the potential benefits of completing the project.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

You are looking for documentation that includes the analysis of the ability to complete the
project successfully. The feasibility study is the economic evaluation of the potential benefits of
and the justification for the project. This information is documented in the project business case.
The feasibility study, which establishes the validity of the benefits of completing the project, also
serves as the basis for the authorization of the project and project management activities.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Bid documents**
Incorrect. Bid documents are used to solicit proposals from prospective sellers during
procurement planning. Based on the scenario described, the project has not even yet been
initiated.
- **B Feasibility study**
Correct. The information sought in this question would be found in the feasibility study,
which is documented in the project business case. The feasibility study is used to establish
the validity of the benefits of completing the project and is the basis for authorization of
project management activities.
- **C Plausibility study**
Incorrect. 'Plausibility study' is a fake term made up for this question.
- **D Needs assessment**
Incorrect. A needs assessment generally precedes the feasibility study and does not analyze
the validity of the benefits of completing the project. The needs assessment involves
understanding the business goals and objectives, issues, and opportunities in offering
proposals to address them.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 77-78, 29

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 92 of 200
Question ID: 613278
An internal project is almost complete. The project manager wants to have a final meeting with
the sponsor to discuss how to maximize the value of the deliverables after the project’s
deliverable is deployed.
What does the project manager use to back up the conversation with the sponsor?
- **A The benefits management plan**
- **B The project charter**
- **C The business case**
- **D The activity list**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which document might cover post-deployment activities?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The benefits management plan is the documented explanation defining the processes for
creating, maximizing, and sustaining the benefits provided by a project. The benefits
management plan defines how the deliverables should be maintained, so the deliverables can
provide the highest benefit after they are delivered and not under the purview of the project. The
incorrect answer choices are not likely to have post-deployment information. Therefore, of the
choices provided, the benefits management plan is the best response.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A The benefits management plan**
Correct. The benefits management plan defines how the customer must maintain the
deliverables, so the deliverables provide the highest benefit after they are delivered and not
under the purview of the project.
- **B The project charter**
Incorrect. The project charter may have high-level project description, boundaries, and key
deliverables, but it does not have detailed information for when the deliverables are in an
operational state.
- **C The business case**
Incorrect. The business case has the cost justification for the project, but it does not contain
what needs to be done after the project is complete and the deliverables are in an
operational state.
- **D The activity list**
Incorrect. The activity list is a documented tabulation of schedule activities that shows the
activity description, activity identifier, and a sufficiently detailed scope of work description,
so project team members understand what work is to be performed. The activity list does
not likely have information regarding deliverables post-deployment.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 33, 125

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 93 of 200
Question ID: 612743
You are managing a large manufacturing pilot project with extensive and highly detailed quality
requirements. During planning, it is determined that there will be a high volume of quality
control measurements being captured by a fully automated system.
Which of the following would you likely use as a guideline on how and where this data be stored
and processed?
- **A Quality management system**
- **B Test and evaluation documents**
- **C Work performance reports**
- **D Quality management register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Due to the high volume of measurements being captured, an automated repository will be
necessary.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

According to the scenario, a high volume of quality control measurements will be captured. This
implies the project will be in the Control Quality process. Most organizations with complex
quality requirements implement an automated, enterprise-level quality management system. This
is the organizational framework whose structure provides the policies, processes, procedures, and
resources required to implement the quality management program. The typical project quality
management plan should be compatible with the organization’s quality management system. This
system may include, for example, a description of a database component that will continuously
store and process quality control measurements collected during carrying out the Control Quality
process.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Quality management system**
Correct. The quality management system is the organizational framework whose structure
provides the policies, processes, procedures, and resources required to implement the
quality management plan. The system may include, for example, guidelines on how and
where the quality control measurements captured during the Control Quality process
should be stored and processed.
- **B Test and evaluation documents**
Incorrect. Test and evaluation documents are project documents that describe quality
activities. Those documents do not provide guidelines on how and where the quality control
measurements should be stored or processed.
- **C Work performance reports**
Incorrect. Work performance reports are the physical or electronic representation of work
performance information compiled in project documents. While these reports will likely
contain some quality control measurements, this is not the place to document guidelines on
storage and processing those measurements.
- **D Quality management register**
Incorrect. 'Quality management register' is a made-up term.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 718, 305, 281

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 94 of 200
Question ID: 651020
You are managing a web and mobile software application development project using an agile
approach, planning an early iteration of work. In the table shown, you have a list of risk user
stories to add to the risk-adjusted product backlog.
Which of the following would not be among the top three risks?
- **A Compatibility issues with beta Windows Phone**
- **B Compatibility issues with beta Apple iOS**
- **C Integration issues with beta United release**
- **D Compatibility issues with beta Android OS**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

To rank the risks, find the basic expected monetary value for each one. The risks with the highest
EMV have the highest priority to address first.
Correct Answer: C

---


**Explanation:**

Expected Monetary Value is the expected financial loss or gain associated with project risks. It is
the product of a risk's probability and impact (EMV=P*I). To rank the risks, you would find the
EMV for each risk. The risks with the highest EMV have the highest priority to address first.
In the table below, the EMV for each risk is calculated in the last column. In this case, the two
risks that would not be among the top three are "Integration issues with the beta Sabre release"
and "Integration issues with the beta United release." Therefore, the answer is "Integration issues
with the beta United release."

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Compatibility issues with beta Windows Phone**
Incorrect. The EMV for this risk is 3600, which the top EMV for this list.
- **B Compatibility issues with beta Apple iOS**
Incorrect. The EMV for this risk is 3000, which is among the top three EMVs.
- **C Integration issues with beta United release**
Correct. The EMV for this risk is 2500, which is not among the top three EMVs.
- **D Compatibility issues with beta Android OS**
Incorrect. The EMV for this risk is 3200, which is among the top three EMVs.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page 400; see
also https://www.projectmanagement.com/articles/341541/Agile-Risk-Management

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 95 of 200
Question ID: 613764
- **A project manager has been informed that an identified risk comes from a questionable source.**
After further investigation, the project manager realizes that the risk was based on an article
where the author never cited any sources, has no experience in the industry, and has been
contradicted by credible industry experts. The risk will have to be reassessed.
What risk analysis technique did the project manager use?
- **A Risk data quality assessment**
- **B Document analysis**
- **C Risk probability and impact assessment**
- **D Expert judgment**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What technique can be used to evaluate the degree to which the data about individual project
risks is accurate and reliable as a basis for qualitative risk analysis?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

This is an example of risk data quality assessment – a data analysis technique used as part of the
Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process. The project manager is evaluating the degree to
which the risk data is accurate and credible, specifically by assessing the quality of the magazine
article as a data source. Since the use of low-quality risk data can lead to a qualitative risk
analysis that is of little value to the project, the project manager has realized that it may be
necessary to gather better data and reassess the risk.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Risk data quality assessment**
Correct. Risk data quality assessment evaluates the degree to which the risk data is
accurate and reliable. The identified risk came from an article that may have been based on
the subjective views and predictions of an author with low credibility.
- **B Document analysis**
Incorrect. Document analysis is a technique used in the Identify Risks process. This
technique involves reviewing internal project documents, including project plans, previous
project files, contracts, and technical documentation, in order to find indicators of risk on
the project.
- **C Risk probability and impact assessment**
Incorrect. The risk probability and impact assessment is an example of data analysis
techniques that can be used in qualitative risk analysis. However, in the scenario, the
project manager is not considering the probability and impact of this particular risk, but
rather evaluating the accuracy and credibility of the risk data upon which this risk is based
– a technique known as risk data quality assessment.
- **D Expert judgment**
Incorrect. Although arguably the project manager is using a form of expert judgment to
conduct this risk data quality assessment, this is not the primary technique described in the
scenario. The specific actions taken by the project manager closely follow the definition of
risk data quality assessment.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 423, 415, 422

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 96 of 200
Question ID: 612169
You are managing a project to relocate a historic building to a new property that is a safe distance
from the rising river basin. You have just finished developing your cost estimate, and are
preparing the supporting documentation to accompany it.
What should be included in this documentation?
- **A Cost register**
- **B Cost forecast**
- **C Range of possible estimates**
- **D Cost baseline**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What information is included in the basis of estimates used to support the cost estimate?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Based on the scenario described, your project is in planning, and you are performing the
Estimate Costs process. One of the outputs from the Estimate Costs process is the basis of
estimates. It provides a clear and complete understanding of how the cost estimate was derived
and is supporting documentation for the cost estimate. Also included in the supporting details, is
documentation of all assumptions made, any known constraints, and an indication of the range of
possible estimates (e.g., $100,000 +/- 10%) to show the cost is within a range of values.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Cost register**
Incorrect. 'Cost register' is a fake term made up for this question.
- **B Cost forecast**
Incorrect. A cost forecast is a calculation derived from earned value analysis to monitor
how well the project is comparing to the cost baseline. It is used in controlling costs, not
estimating them making this choice an incorrect answer.
- **C Range of possible estimates**
Correct. The range of possible estimates is one of the supporting details included with the
cost estimates.
- **D Cost baseline**
Incorrect. The cost baseline is the approved version of the time-phased project budget. It is
used as a basis for comparison to actual results to control the project budget. The cost
baseline is used in the controlling processes of a project and not to support an estimate.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 247

PMP Exam 5
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 97 of 200
Question ID: 612163
As a project manager, you are leading the effort to construct the cellular towers. Another project
manager is in charge of building the data center, and yet another project manager is heading up
the development of retail distribution. All three of the projects are being managed in a
coordinated manner.
For which of the following might you be responsible?
- **A Assuring benefits realization from the program and component projects**
- **B Capturing lessons learned, which may benefit other program components**
- **C Managing interdependencies between program components**
- **D Managing change requests within a shared governance framework**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Program components consist of individual projects that are being managed as a group.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Program components consist of individual projects that are being managed in a coordinated
manner. In this case, the three individual projects are components of a program. Program
management focuses on the interdependencies between projects to determine the optimal
approach for managing them. All the incorrect answer choices represent interdependencies,
which must be addressed at the program rather than the project level.
Important lessons learned should be captured in the lessons learned register and then transferred
to the lessons learned repository. These lessons learned may improve the performance of the
current project, other component projects, or future projects. However, the identification and
recording of lessons learned is the responsibility of each project manager. Therefore, of the

---

available choices, capturing lessons learned which may benefit other program components is the
best answer.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Assuring benefits realization from the program and component projects**
Incorrect. Individual project managers are responsible for obtaining project objectives
leading to the realization of project benefits. Program benefits are beyond the realm for
individual project managers and are the responsibility of the program manager.
- **B Capturing lessons learned, which may benefit other program components**
Correct. Lessons learned may improve the performance of the current project, other
component projects, or future projects. However, the identification and recording of lessons
learned is the responsibility of each project manager.
- **C Managing interdependencies between program components**
Incorrect. When projects are managed as a program, inter-dependencies likely exist among
the projects. In this scenario, the retail distribution is dependent upon the cellular coverage
area. These inter-dependencies must be managed at the program level and not by the
managers of the individual projects.
- **D Managing change requests within a shared governance framework**
Incorrect. When projects are managed as a program, changes to one project may affect
other projects within the program. For example, a change request to update the schedule
baseline for one project may impact the timeline of one or more of the other component
projects. Therefore, a project manager may submit a change request for their project, but
the change must be managed at the program level.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 14
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next
