Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 147 of 200
Question ID: 651355
Due to a labor shortage, the project has endured an increase in costs for recruiting and hiring.
Production has slowed considerably, and the original budget is unachievable.
With the sponsor willing to invest more money, what should be used to determine the rate at
which the project team needs to perform work to meet the original delivery date?
Top of Form
- **A TCPI using the adjusted EAC**
- **B TCPI using the BAC**
- **C CPI using the adjusted EAC**
- **D SPI using the BAC**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Is the original budget viable?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

As the project progresses, the actual results are analyzed against the planned results via the
earned value analysis (EVA). At any point in the project, the to-complete performance index
(TCPI) can be used to determine the ratio at which the work should be completed in order to
meet the target. The target at first is the budget at completion (BAC). In this scenario, that target
is considered no longer achievable. Hence, the project team must perform at a rate that meets the
new adjusted budget - designated by the estimate at completion (EAC). Using the equation for
TCPI that involves the EAC is what the team needs to determine that rate of performance:

---

TCPI = (BAC - EV) / (EAC - AC)
Note, to answer this question correctly, no calculation, but the understanding of the TCPI and its
interpretation is required. The formula is provided for your reference.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A TCPI using the adjusted EAC**
Correct. The original budget at completion is no longer viable. The project has a new
estimate. That new adjusted estimate at completion is what the team must use to determine
the rate of performance necessary to reach that new target. The TCPI using the EAC
determines that ratio.
- **B TCPI using the BAC**
Incorrect. The original budget at completion is no longer viable. The project has a new
estimate. That estimate, not the original target, must be in the TCPI equation to determine
the performance rate for the remainder of the project.
- **C CPI using the adjusted EAC**
Incorrect. The cost performance index (CPI) is a measure of the cost efficiency that has
been achieved by the project up until the point the CPI has been calculated. However, in
this scenario, the team must determine the future (not past) cost performance required to
meet the project objectives.
- **D SPI using the BAC**
Incorrect. The schedule performance index (SPI) is a measure of the schedule efficiency
that has been achieved by the project up until the point the SPI has been calculated.
However, in this scenario, the team must determine the future (not past) cost performance
required to meet the project objectives.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 266-268
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 148 of 200
Question ID: 651316
- **A project is looking to procure a series of products to be developed in tandem with the project. A**
single supplier must be able to build out the products and provide services to the project team as
the team works on the multitude of other components.
To best manage the quality of the long-term procurement need, what is the best practice?
Top of Form
- **A Require the seller to deliver earlier than needed to accommodate repairs of poor quality**
deliverables
- **B Reduce the number of metrics to optimize the cost of quality and associated assets**
- **C Tighten the quality standards at various points in the project to ensure the seller is staying aware**
of changing conditions
- **D Form a relationship with the seller to build cooperation and mutually lasting solutions**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is the best arrangement between the project team and the supplier?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

An emerging best practice for quality management is cooperating with suppliers rather than
having it be a unidirectional transaction. This is especially beneficial in situations, like in this
question, where the project team and the selected seller must work in tandem to develop a series
of products and the underpinning services. Establishing a partnership with the supplier is a good
practice. Setting and maintaining a certain set of quality standards for a project and the project's

---

procurement needs over the length of the project is essential to ensure constant and reliable
quality and healthy working relationships with the seller.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Require the seller to deliver earlier than needed to accommodate repairs of poor quality**
deliverables
Incorrect. The assumption should not be that the seller is to constantly provide poor quality
or incomplete work. The project team and the supplier must work together to ensure the
requirements and the quality standards are understood and adhered to. Forcing the seller
to deliver early with the assumption the deliverables do not meet expectations erodes trust
between buyer and seller.
- **B Reduce the number of metrics to optimize the cost of quality and associated assets**
Incorrect. Reducing the measurements and quality metrics does not increase quality
without a compelling reason as to why and how. Metrics are a means to check and assure
quality. Conducting fewer checks does not equate to higher quality.
- **C Tighten the quality standards at various points in the project to ensure the seller is staying**
aware of changing conditions
Incorrect. Tightening quality standards at selected points may be needed, as long as all
parties are cognizant of those changes and why those standards fall within the terms and
conditions of the agreement. Changing the standards to see if the seller is staying aware of
conditions is not an effective buyer-seller relationship.
- **D Form a relationship with the seller to build cooperation and mutually lasting solutions**
Correct. The project is in need of many products and services from a selected seller.
Developing a mutually beneficial relationship and understanding of the procurement needs
over the course of the project improves cooperation and promotes understanding of shared
goals and quality standards.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 275

PMP Exam 5

Question 149 of 200
Question ID: 612980
Your project is to design a payroll automation system for a client company. You have assured the
client that the system contains all of the state-of-the-art features to protect it against modern
threats. The client has asked you to perform a penetration test in order to validate your claim.
The cost to perform this test is an example of which of the following?
Top of Form
- **A Cost plus fixed fee**
- **B Cost of changes**
- **C Cost of nonconformance**
- **D Cost of conformance**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Paying for the penetration test would help you avoid failure to satisfy a customer requirement.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Penetration testing is a technique to test the deterrence of a system against hacking attempts. This
technique is typically a costly activity and requires time and expertise. Testing is performed to
assess the quality of a system and is considered appraisal costs. Appraisal costs fall under the
cost of conformance category and are an example of the data analysis techniques that can be used
as part of the Plan Quality Management process.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Cost plus fixed fee**
Incorrect. Cost plus fixed fee is a type of cost-reimbursable procurement contract where the
client pays for allowable expenses as well as a fee that does not change, being based on a
percentage of the original estimated project costs. The cost to perform a penetration test is
not an example of a contract.
- **B Cost of changes**
Incorrect. Cost of changes refers to the cost of making changes and correcting errors
throughout a project life cycle. The cost of the penetration test is not related to changes or
errors.
- **C Cost of nonconformance**
Incorrect. It would be considered the cost of non-conformance if the system had already
failed such that you may incur cost for rework or scrapping work if the failures were found
by the project. Non-conformance may also include additional liabilities, warranty work or
lost business if the failures were found by the customer. The penetration test requested by
the customer does not fall under any of these categories, making the cost of
nonconformance an incorrect answer.
- **D Cost of conformance**
Correct. Penetration testing is an appraisal cost to assess the quality of the work product. It
is money spent to avoid failure in satisfying customer requirements. This falls under the
cost of conformance.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 283

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 150 of 200
Question ID: 613730
Which of the following represents a point in the project life cycle where stakeholder
identification can take place?
Top of Form
- **A Initiation, planning, execution, monitoring and controlling, and closure**
- **B Initiation only**
- **C Initiation and planning**
- **D Planning and execution**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Is the process of identifying stakeholders restricted to one process group?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The process of identifying stakeholders is frequently performed for the first time during the
initiation of the project. However, if any point in the project, a person, group, or organization is
found to affect, or be affected by, the project, they should be identified as a stakeholder and
analyzed as to their impact of the project. Therefore, choosing the choice that includes all points
in the project life cycle is the best answer. Note, the question is not about a Process Group or
Domain in which stakeholder identification can take place. The question is about a point in a
project life cycle. While the names look similar, they are not the same.
One may argue that identifying stakeholders during project closure makes little sense. While it is
true that towards the end of the project the chances of identifying a new stakeholder are low, it
does not mean that new stakeholders should be ignored. Project closure consists of many

---

activities. It is possible that a newly identified stakeholder is supposed to take over the project
deliverables to operate and support them in production. If for some reason this stakeholder was
not identified on time and ignored during project closure, it is likely that such a stakeholder may
become resistant, stall the handover process, and negatively affect project closure. Another
example is a multi-phase project. What if the newly identified stakeholder is supposed to be part
of the next phase?

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Initiation, planning, execution, monitoring and controlling, and closure**
Correct. Stakeholders can be identified at any time during the project. The formal process
of Identify Stakeholders is performed as part of the Initiating Process Group. However, at
any point in the project, if a person, group, or organization is found to affect, or be affected
by, the project, they are identified as a stakeholder.
- **B Initiation only**
Incorrect. Frequently, the process of identifying stakeholders is done during the initiation of
the project at the same time as the project charter is being written and approved. However,
at any point in the project, if a person, group, or organization is found to affect, or be
affected by, the project, they are identified as a stakeholder. Therefore, this is not the best
answer.
- **C Initiation and planning**
Incorrect. Frequently, the process of identifying stakeholders is done during the initiation of
the project at the same time as the project charter is being written and approved. However,
a stakeholder can be identified during any point in the project life cycle. Therefore, this
choice represent an incorrect answer.
- **D Planning and execution**
Incorrect. The process of identifying stakeholders is done during the initiation of the
project. However, anytime a person, group, or organization is found to be affected by the
project they should be identified as a stakeholder. This answer does not include project
initiation, making this choice an incomplete answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 507-508, 19
Bottom of Form

Question 151 of 200
Question ID: 610023
After checking the internal resources, the project manager realizes that the company does not
have developers who are experienced in the programming language required for the project.
What should the project manager do next?
Top of Form
- **A Build a virtual team with internal resources**
- **B Recommend terminating the project**
- **C Acquire the resources externally**
- **D Seek help from the project sponsor**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

If the company does not have the required internal resources, the project manager may need to
look outside the organization.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project manager is performing the Acquire Resources process. The
resources needed for the project can be internal or external to the project-performing
organization. However, in the scenario described by the question, the performing organization
lacks developers experienced with the required programming language. Therefore, of the choices
provided, the logical action for the project manager is to acquire the resources from outside the
organization.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Build a virtual team with internal resources**
Incorrect. The use of a virtual team opens up new possibilities when acquiring project team
members by forming a team of people from the same organization who are located in broad
geographic areas. However, the question states that the company does not have any
developers internally with experience in the required programming language. Therefore,
regardless of whether the team is collocated or virtual, using internal resources will not
resolve the problem described in the question.
- **B Recommend terminating the project**
Incorrect. Terminating the project just because the company lacks the internal resources to
complete the project work is an over-reaction. The project manager may consider acquiring
the resources externally. Therefore, this answer choice can be eliminated.
- **C Acquire the resources externally**
Correct. The resources needed for the project can be internal or external to the
project-performing organization. When the performing organization lacks the resources
necessary to perform project work, the resource can be acquired externally, typically
through the procurement processes.
- **D Seek help from the project sponsor**
Incorrect. There are many tools and techniques available at the disposition of the project
manager to acquire resources. Escalating the issue to the project sponsor is a premature
action.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 329-330

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 152 of 200
Question ID: 651315
- **A project team member has left the project and company. The replacement needs to get up to**
speed quickly and determine what work packages and activities are assigned to her team and
department.
Which of the following should she reference?
Top of Form
- **A The project management office**
- **B The organizational breakdown structure**
- **C The project organization chart**
- **D The organizational process assets**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Is it the work she needs to reference or where in the organization the work is assigned?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The organizational breakdown structure (OBS) is an example of the hierarchical chart that can be
used as a data representation technique while carrying out the Plan Resource Management
process. The OBS presents the work packages and activities and how they are aligned with the
organizational units of a project or company, such as team, department, and business unit.
Therefore, the new team member should refer to the OBS to determine what work packages and
activities are assigned to her team and department.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The project management office**
Incorrect. The project management office (PMO) is an organizational structure that
standardizes the project-related governance processes and facilitates the sharing of
resources, methodologies, tools, and techniques. Depending on its type (supportive,
controlling, or directive), the PMO may provide direction to the project team on project
management and organizational assets, but not the project activities assigned to an
organizational unit.
- **B The organizational breakdown structure**
Correct. The organizational breakdown structure (OBS) shows the work packages and/or
activities according to the organization’s departments, teams, or forms of division. The OBS
is the best reference for the new team member to learn which responsibilities are assigned
to her team and department.
- **C The project organization chart**
Incorrect. A project organization chart is a graphic display of the project team and their
reporting relationships. While this would help the new team member determine who she is
reporting to in the project, it would not list what work packages and activities are assigned
to her team and department.
- **D The organizational process assets**
Incorrect. The organizational process assets (OPA) are the plans, processes, policies,
procedures, and knowledge bases specific to and used by the performing organization.
There may be an OPA to help the team create an OBS. However, the OPAs do not specify
what work packages and activities are assigned to the teams and departments within the
organization.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 316

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 153 of 200
Question ID: 612321
- **A software development team implemented pair programming as a risk response. In a subsequent**
risk review, it was determined to be highly effective in catching programming errors and
dramatically reducing the number of escaped defects.
As a result of the risk review meeting, what should the project manager do first?
Top of Form
- **A Submit a change request to update the risk management plan**
- **B Notify the project management office (PMO) of results from the risk review meeting**
- **C Capture the information in the lessons learned register**
- **D Update the lessons learned repository with the knowledge gained**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which project document should be updated with knowledge gained during a project?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

- **A risk review meeting is conducted as part of the Monitor Risks process. The question describes**
knowledge gained in the form of an effective risk response as the result of the risk review
meeting. The lessons learned register is updated with any risk-related lessons learned during risk
reviews so the knowledge gained can be used in later phases of the project. At the end of the
project, the information contained in the lessons learned register is transferred to the lessons
learned repository for use on future projects. Therefore, of the available options, capturing the
information in the lessons learned register is the best answer to the question asked.

---

Pair programming is a coding technique that is often used on agile projects. While this
knowledge is not needed to answer this question correctly, it is important to understand that some
projects can be managed using a hybrid project management approach where the project as a
whole is lead using traditional management while some of its elements are carried out using agile
methods.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Submit a change request to update the risk management plan**
Incorrect. The question describes knowledge gained as the result of a risk review meeting,
which is not captured in the risk management plan. Additionally, the implementation of an
agreed-upon risk response should not require a modification to the risk management plan.
- **B Notify the project management office (PMO) of results from the risk review meeting**
Incorrect. Company policy or best practices may or may not include notifying the PMO of
the results from risk review meetings. Regardless, it is best first to capture the knowledge
gained described by the question in the lessons learned register, which can then be shared
with the PMO if needed.
- **C Capture the information in the lessons learned register**
Correct. A risk review meeting is conducted as part of the Monitor Risks process. Any
knowledge gained as a result of the risk review meeting should be captured in the lessons
learned register.
- **D Update the lessons learned repository with the knowledge gained**
Incorrect. Knowledge gained during the risk review meeting should first be captured in the
lessons learned register. As part of the Close Project or Phase process, the information
from the lessons learned register is then transferred to the lessons learned repository as an
organizational process asset, where it can be used as an input for future projects to improve
performance.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 458

PMP Exam 5

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 154 of 200
Question ID: 626029
Midway into project execution, you have been asked to shorten your project duration by three
weeks to meet a new deadline but deliver all originally planned functionality. Additional
resources are available, and the cost is not as great a concern as schedule.
What should you do?
Top of Form
- **A Crash activities on the critical path**
- **B Remove external dependencies**
- **C Reduce project scope**
- **D Level resources**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which of the following is the schedule compression technique?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Provided that resources are available and an increase in cost is acceptable, to shorten your project
schedule you can use a schedule compression technique such as crashing. Crashing is adding
resources to an activity in order to complete it earlier than scheduled. This technique is typically
used during project planning as part of the Develop Schedule process. While the scenario implies
the project is already in execution, crashing can still be used as this technique is not limited only
to the planning stage of the project. Project planning is an iterative process and can be done as
necessary. Note, an approved change request will be required to crash the activities on the critical

---

path as the implication of this action would likely affect some of the components of the project
management plan.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Crash activities on the critical path**
Correct. Crashing is a schedule compression technique that can be used to shorten the
overall project schedule. Given the information that resources are available and the cost
was not a great concern relative to time, crashing the activities on the critical path is the
best choice.
- **B Remove external dependencies**
Incorrect. Removing external dependencies is not always possible as they are often outside
the project team's control. Even if possible, removing external dependencies does not
guarantee the project can be finished earlier.
- **C Reduce project scope**
Incorrect. While reducing scope may result in shortening the duration of the project,
according to the scenario, the project should deliver all originally planned functionality.
Therefore, reducing the project scope is not an option.
- **D Level resources**
Incorrect. Resource leveling will not shorten the project and could actually lengthen the
project if a resource is over-allocated.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 215, 211-212, 191-193
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 155 of 200
Question ID: 625049
- **A project is underway, and only the baselines and project management plan are captured in the**
configuration management plan. A key stakeholder has submitted a formal request to include a
new requirement in your project. The change would affect many project constraints. It increases
the risk of the project going over budget and behind schedule. The change request has been
approved by the change control board (CCB), and you have updated the scope baseline.
What should you do next?
Top of Form
- **A Modify the stakeholder's classification in the stakeholder register**
- **B Deny the request to avoid scope creep and keep your project on track**
- **C Record the attributes of the new requirement in the requirements traceability matrix**
- **D Submit a change request for an update to the requirements documentation**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which project document may be updated as the result of a newly identified stakeholder
requirement?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The requirements traceability matrix is a grid that links product requirements from their origin to
the deliverables that satisfy them. Updates to the requirements traceability matrix are among the
outputs of the Control Scope process described in the question. Attributes associated with each
requirement can be recorded in the requirements traceability matrix. These attributes help to
define key information about the requirement. Among the available choices, recording the

---

attributes associated with the stakeholder requirement in the requirements traceability matrix is
the best answer to the question asked.
Note, the question states that the change will affect many project constraints. The project is at
greater risk of being over budget and behind schedule. Since the change request has been
approved, one would expect the project manager to update all three baselines (scope, schedule,
cost). However, according to the scenario, the project manager updated only the scope baseline.
The absence of this information does not change the correct answer. PMP aspirants should
expect some questions on the real exam to be incomplete, and, therefore, make reasonable
assumptions based on the information available in the question, and, of the choices provided,
select the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Modify the stakeholder's classification in the stakeholder register**
Incorrect. The stakeholder register may document each stakeholders' classification such as
internal/external or impact/influence/power/interest, etc. The question does not suggest that
a stakeholder's classification has changed. Therefore, modifying the stakeholder's
classification in the stakeholder register is not required.
- **B Deny the request to avoid scope creep and keep your project on track**
Incorrect. Scope creep is defined as the uncontrolled expansion of product or project scope
without adjustments to time, cost, and resources. Even though the change will affect many
project constraints and even risk to put the project over budget and behind schedule, the
question states that the requested change was approved by the CCB, implying the change is
not uncontrolled, and that all constraints have been considered. Additionally, the project
manager is not likely to have the authority to override a decision made by the CCB.
- **C Record the attributes of the new requirement in the requirements traceability matrix**
Correct. The requirements traceability matrix is a grid that links product requirements from
their origin to the deliverables that satisfy them. The question indicates that a stakeholder
requirement has been added to the project. Therefore, the requirements traceability matrix
should be updated to include the attributes associated with the new requirement.
- **D Submit a change request for an update to the requirements documentation**
Incorrect. The new requirement should be included in the requirements documentation.
However, the question states that only the baselines and project management plan are
captured in the configuration management plan. The requirements documentation is a

---

project document. Therefore, a change request is not required to update the requirements
documentation in this situation.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 171, 148-149

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 156 of 200
Question ID: 625048
During the execution of a project, a change request is submitted and approved.
Which of the following should be done next?
Top of Form
- **A Holding a meeting to review the change requests that have been approved**
- **B Analyzing the impact of the requested change on project constraints**
- **C Implementing the change in the Monitor and Control Project Work process**
- **D Updating the status of the change request in the change log**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is an output of the Perform Integrated Change Control process that is then used as an input
to the Direct and Manage Project Work process?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The scenario in the questions describes the submission and approval of a change request
implying the Perform Integrated Change Control process has been carried out. The change log
has to be updated to reflect the change was approved and other information about the change that
may affect its implementation in the Direct and Manage Project Work process. According to the
reference provided, Figure 4-13 on page 114, it can be seen that the change log is updated as an
output of the Perform Integrated Change Control process. Similarly, by reviewing the data flow
diagram for the Direct and Manage Project Work process, one can see that the change log is

---

shown as an input into that process. Thus, the change log must be revised before implementing
any change.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Holding a meeting to review the change requests that have been approved**
Incorrect. There is indeed a meeting called approved change requests review. This type of
meeting is held as part of the Control Quality process and aimed to verify that the changes
have been implemented as approved. According to the scenario, the change has just been
approved. The change should first be implemented before its implementation can be
verified.
- **B Analyzing the impact of the requested change on project constraints**
Incorrect. As part of the Perform Integrated Change Control process, the change request is
analyzed for its potential impact on the project and the project constraints. The question
states that the change request has been approved, implying an impact analysis has already
occurred.
- **C Implementing the change in the Monitor and Control Project Work process**
Incorrect. The work approved in the change request will be implemented in the Direct and
Manage Project Work process, not in the Monitor and Control Project Work process, which
is the process of tracking, reviewing, and reporting overall progress to meet the
performance objectives defined in the project management plan.
- **D Updating the status of the change request in the change log**
Correct. The change log documents all changes on the project and is the source for both
approved and denied change requests. At all points in the project, the change log reflects
the disposition or status of all changes requests for the project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 120, 91-92, 113-114
Bottom of Form

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 157 of 200
Question ID: 612541
- **A project has been initiated to build a facility next to an estate with a homeowner association**
(HOA). During the first meeting with the HOA representatives, the project manager listened but
did not directly address their concerns that the facility would be noisy and an eyesore. When they
next met, the two parties cooperatively worked towards an agreement for the project to plant
trees to obstruct the view and reduce the noise of the storage facility.
What best describes interactions of the project manager with the HOA?
Top of Form
- **A Implement Risk Responses**
- **B Meeting management**
- **C Avoidance and collaboration**
- **D Alternatives selection**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

There are five techniques for managing conflict.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

In the scenario, the project manager is conducting the Develop Project Charter process. Conflict
management is one of the tools and techniques of that process. Conflict management can be used
to help bring stakeholders into alignment on the elements of the project charter. During the first
meeting with the stakeholders, the project manager listens to their concerns but avoids the
conflict because she is unprepared to address it. In other words, the project manager used the
conflict management technique of withdraw/avoid. A follow-up meeting with the stakeholders

---

represents a collaborate/problem solve conflict management technique where the parties agree on
a win-win solution acceptable to both sides. Avoidance and collaboration are both represented in
the scenario making avoidance and collaboration the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Implement Risk Responses**
Incorrect. Implement Risk Responses is the executing process of performing agreed-upon
activities when an identified risk has occurred. The project is in the initiating stage, making
this choice an incorrect answer.
- **B Meeting management**
Incorrect. Meeting management is an interpersonal skill that involves planning, executing,
and follow up of meetings so they are productive. The scenario describes meetings with the
homeowners' association; however, the focus is on the outcome of the meetings and not the
management of the meetings.
- **C Avoidance and collaboration**
Correct. Withdraw/avoid and collaborate/problem solve are among interpersonal skills that
can be used as tools and techniques to manage conflicts. The question focuses on a conflict
that has been resolved by the project manager who applied their interpersonal skills to
ensure project stakeholders agree on the project charter. Therefore, of the choices provided,
avoidance and collaboration is the best answer to the question asked.
- **D Alternatives selection**
Incorrect. 'Alternatives selection' is a made-up term for this question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 80, 348-349

PMP Exam 5

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 158 of 200
Question ID: 613795
You are managing a project where several key stakeholders feel it is a risky project. Your
variance analysis shows you have a negative project float. Your CPI is 1.3. You and your project
management team are discussing ways to bring the schedule back into alignment with the project
management plan.
Which of the following schedule-shortening options would be the best option?
Top of Form
- **A Crash the project**
- **B Fast track the project**
- **C Reduce the scope**
- **D Lower the quality standards**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which schedule compression technique would be best to use when your project is under budget?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

If your project has negative project float, the estimated completion date will be after the desired
completion date. You and your project management team are looking for ways to reduce the
schedule and bring it back into alignment with the project plan. In determining a path forward,
you need to look at all the potential options for reducing the schedule and choose the option with
the least impact on the project. The scenario implies that some of the key stakeholders have low
risk tolerances, and fast tracking usually adds risk. Reducing scope or lowering quality will

---

reduce the project schedule but will most likely negatively impact the customer. The project is
under budget, however, so crashing the project is the best choice.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Crash the project**
Correct. Crashing the project is a technique used to shorten the project schedule by adding
resources. Crashing can be accomplished by approving overtime or bringing in additional
resources. Crashing a project always involves increased cost, but according to the CPI of
1.3, the project is operating under budget. Therefore, of the choices provided, this is the
best solution.
- **B Fast track the project**
Incorrect. Fast tracking a project is a technique used to shorten the project schedule.
Activities that are usually completed in the sequence are performed in parallel. Fast
tracking a project may result in increased risk and rework. Since some of your key
stakeholders feel the project is already risky, increasing the risk would not be the best
choice for schedule compression in this scenario. Therefore, this is not the best answer.
- **C Reduce the scope**
Incorrect. Reducing the scope would likely reduce the schedule variance; however, it
cannot be done unilaterally. Even if the customer agreed to reduce the scope, the scope
reduction would most likely negatively impact customers' satisfaction. Therefore, reducing
the scope would not be the best option.
- **D Lower the quality standards**
Incorrect. Quality is a project constraint. Therefore, lowering quality would most likely
reduce the schedule variance. However, it also reasonable to assume that lowering the
quality standards will negatively impact customers' satisfaction. Therefore, this choice is an
incorrect answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 228, 215
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam 5

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 159 of 200
Question ID: 613657
- **A project team on a construction project have updated the risk register and risk report. One of the**
high-priority risks is a major hurricane that may occur during construction and could potentially
result in massive rework.
What should the project manager do next to determine whether or not hurricane barriers should
be built as a preventive measure?
Top of Form
- **A Evaluate the risk breakdown structure (RBS) to figure out if a hurricane is a risk the project is**
willing to accept.
- **B Conduct a decision tree analysis to quantify the expense of building hurricane barriers versus the**
expense of rework.
- **C Conduct a probability and impact assessment to determine where the hurricane risk ranks in**
relational to other risks.
- **D Produce risk scores to assess the likelihood a major hurricane will occur during the construction**
time frame.
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Cost is usually a deciding factor in evaluating project risk.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The RBS can be ruled out as a correct answer because it is a categorization technique and does
not help the project manager decide between alternative options. The probability and impact
matrix is an output from the Plan Risk Management process. The matrix is then used in the risk

---

probability and impact assessment tool/technique in the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis
process but is unlikely to help the project manager in determining whether or not hurricane
barriers should be built. Risk scores are used to rank risks in the probability and impact matrix
and are also of little value in making a decision regarding building the barriers. The fact the
hurricane risk has already been identified and ranked means the Plan Risk Management, the
Identify Risks, and the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis processes have already been
completed. Therefore, the three answer choices concerning the RBS, the risk scores, and risk
assessment can be eliminated.
The next process in the Project Risk Management Knowledge Area is Perform Quantitative Risk
Analysis. Decision tree analysis is one of its tools and techniques. In deciding whether to build or
not to build the hurricane barriers, cost should be taken into account. A decision tree analysis
calculates the expected monetary value for each alternative, providing quantitative values that
factor into the decision-making process and is, therefore, the best answer choice to the question
asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Evaluate the risk breakdown structure (RBS) to figure out if a hurricane is a risk the**
project is willing to accept.
Incorrect. The level of risk a project is willing to accept would be described in the risk
management plan, not in the RBS. The RBS categorizes risks making this choice an
incorrect answer.
- **B Conduct a decision tree analysis to quantify the expense of building hurricane barriers**
versus the expense of rework.
Correct. A decision tree analysis is a technique that can be used to support a selection of
the best several alternative courses of action (paths) and their associated monetary values.
The project manager would want to get a monetary value for each alternative path to help
make the decision on whether to build the barrier walls.
- **C Conduct a probability and impact assessment to determine where the hurricane risk ranks**
in relational to other risks.
Incorrect. Based on the scenario described, the project risks have already been identified
and ranked with the help of the skilled facilitator, and the hurricane risk has been deemed a
high-priority risk. Therefore, conducting another probability and impact assessment would
be a misuse of project resources.
- **D Produce risk scores to assess the likelihood a major hurricane will occur during the**
construction time frame.

---

Incorrect. Calculating risk scores is a common method used to rank project risk in the
probability and impact matrix. The question implies the project risks have already been
ranked, therefore producing risk scores again would be inappropriate. Also, having risk
scores alone without having monetary value for each alternative path (building hurricane
barriers or not) would not help guide decision between the two alternative paths making
this choice an incorrect answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 435
Bottom of Form

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 160 of 200
Question ID: 612291
You are managing a project in which the first deliverables received corrective feedback from the
client, resulting in change requests that have just been approved.
In which of the following project management process groups do you implement these approved
change requests?
Top of Form
- **A Initiating**
- **B Planning**
- **C Executing**
- **D Closing**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Think about which processes have approved change requests as inputs, then determine which
process group you may select as one of these choices.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

There are only three processes that have approved change requests as inputs: Direct and Manage
Project Work, Control Quality, and Control Procurements. The first of these is in the Executing
process group, and that is when you implement approved change requests. The latter two
processes are in the Monitoring and Controlling, where you verify the changes were properly
implemented, but this process group was not one of the choices.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Initiating**
Incorrect. During the Initiating process group, you are preparing a charter, proving the
business case, and identifying stakeholders. A change request is not required for changes to
be implemented in these artifacts until after the project management plan has been
approved and the project baselined.
- **B Planning**
Incorrect. During the planning process group, you are gathering the requirements,
developing the schedule and budget, and documenting the methods your project team will
use to manage the project. A change request is not required for changes to be implemented
in these artifacts until after the project management plan has been approved and the
project baselined.
- **C Executing**
Correct. Approved change requests are inputs to the Direct and Manage Project Work
process, so it is in the Executing process group that you implement the changes.
- **D Closing**
Incorrect. In the Closing process group, the only process is Close Project or Phase.
Approved change requests are not inputs to this process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 93, 114, 301, 496
Bottom of Form

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 161 of 200
Question ID: 612639
As a project manager, you are in the process of working with the project stakeholders to foster
the appropriate level of stakeholder involvement.
Which activity are you least likely to perform in support of this process?
Top of Form
- **A Clarifying and resolving issues that have been identified by the stakeholders**
- **B Developing a matrix that compares current and desired stakeholder engagement levels**
- **C Addressing any risks or potential concerns related to stakeholder engagement**
- **D Managing stakeholder expectations through negotiation and communication**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which activity is associated with the Plan Stakeholder Engagement process instead of the
Manage Stakeholder Engagement process?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process is underway. Manage
Stakeholder Engagement is the process of communicating and working with stakeholders to meet
their needs and expectations, address issues, and foster appropriate stakeholder involvement. The
question is asking for the activity 'least' likely to be performed as part of this process. The
incorrect answer choices all represent activities that should be conducted in support of the
Manage Stakeholder Engagement process. The correct answer choice describes the stakeholder
engagement assessment matrix which is a data representation technique that is used during the
Plan Stakeholder Engagement process. Plan Stakeholder Engagement is the process of

---

developing approaches to involve project stakeholders, based on their needs, expectations,
interests, and potential impact on the project. Of the available choices, the activity 'least' likely to
be performed in this scenario is the development of a matrix that compares current and desired
stakeholder engagement levels.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Clarifying and resolving issues that have been identified by the stakeholders**
Incorrect. During the Manage Stakeholder Engagement process, any project or stakeholder
concerns are documented in the issue log, as well as any assigned action items associated
with managing the issue.
- **B Developing a matrix that compares current and desired stakeholder engagement levels**
Correct. This answer choice describes the stakeholder engagement assessment matrix
which is a data representation technique that is used during the Plan Stakeholder
Engagement process, whereas the question describes the Manage Stakeholder Engagement
process. Therefore, this answer choice represents the activity 'least' likely to be performed
in support of the process described by the scenario and is, therefore, the best answer to the
question asked.
- **C Addressing any risks or potential concerns related to stakeholder engagement**
Incorrect. Risks and potential concerns of stakeholders are addressed as part of the
Manage Stakeholder Engagement process in order to foster the appropriate level of
stakeholder involvement in the project.
- **D Managing stakeholder expectations through negotiation and communication**
Incorrect. Communication skills and interpersonal and team skills, which includes
negotiation, are two of the tools and techniques which may be used during the Manage
Stakeholder Engagement process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 521-522, 524

PMP Exam 5

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 162 of 200
Question ID: 613463
- **A hospital is closing a project that resulted in a new business process for managing oncology**
patients. The hospital realizes that the same process can be used for all its patients, which can
save the hospital thousands of dollars.
Where should this information be captured?
Top of Form
- **A Benefits management plan**
- **B Lessons learned register**
- **C Business case**
- **D Process improvement plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Project document updates are an output of the Close Project or Phase process.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

All project documents may be updated as a result of project closure. Of particular interest is the
lessons learned register which is finalized to include final information on phase or project
closure. The final lessons learned register might include information on benefits management,
the accuracy of the business case, project and development life cycles, risk and issue
management, stakeholder engagement, and other project management processes. The scenario
describes an additional benefit the project created on top of what has been originally planned.

---

This information should be recorded in the lessons learned register and later on transferred to the
lessons learned repository for use by future projects.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Benefits management plan**
Incorrect. The benefits management plan is the documented explanation defining the
processes for creating, maximizing, and sustaining the benefits provided by a project or
program. While the new process is apparently adding more benefits than initially planned,
the benefits management plan is not updated as the result of this realization.
- **B Lessons learned register**
Correct. The lessons learned register is a project document that captures the knowledge
gained during a project. Updates to the lessons learned register is an output of the Close
Project or Phase process described in the scenario. The final lessons learned register might
include information on benefits management, the accuracy of the business case, etc.
- **C Business case**
Incorrect. The business case is a documented economic feasibility study used to establish
the validity of the benefits of a selected component lacking sufficient definition, and that is
used as a basis for the authorization of further project management activities. The business
case is not updated as a result of the knowledge gained throughout the project.
- **D Process improvement plan**
Incorrect. 'Process improvement plan' is not a plan specified in the PMBOK® Guide.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 127

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 163 of 200
Question ID: 613409
One of the project manager's key responsibilities is to motivate the project team to achieve
maximum productivity and increase the probability of project success.
In this respect, according to Maslow's hierarchy of needs, which of the below is most correct?
Top of Form
- **A Physiological needs such as food water and sleep must be met before financial compensation,**
recognition, and social relationships can significantly motivate the team.
- **B All workers fit into two groups, X and Y. The X group avoids responsibility, does the least work**
possible, and requires constant supervision. Those in the Y group are willing to work without close
supervision and want to achieve.
- **C All motivators can be divided into hygiene factors that must be satisfied, such as working**
conditions and salary; and motivating agents such as responsibility and recognition.
- **D There are three universal motivators: achievement, affiliation, and power. In every person, one of**
these three will dominate the other two.
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which motivating factors are the most fundamental?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question refers to organizational theories which should be considered as part of the Plan
Resource Management process. An organizational theory provides information about how
people, teams, and organizational units behave - in this case, the project team. While all answer

---

choices represent various organizational theories, only one describes Maslow's theory of human
motivation. Psychologist Abraham Maslow grouped motivational factors into a hierarchy, with
physiological needs such as air, food, water, and sleep at the lowest and most fundamental level.
He argued that these essential needs must be met before people can be motivated by higher order
factors, such as financial security, recognition, and social acceptance. In order to best motivate
the project team, it is important to ensure that basic needs are indeed met, such as ensuring a
standard work schedule and providing reasonable working conditions.
Although the PMBOK® Guide comprises the majority of the content you will encounter on
your exam, the PMP® Examination Content Outline assumes that the prospective PMP aspirants
are familiar with other sources that are used by the Project Management Institute (PMI)® as
content material. These include such topics as PMI’s Practice Standards, PMI Code of Ethics and
Professional Conduct, PMI’s Practice Standard for Scheduling; commonly accepted statistical
analysis techniques such as ROI, IRR, and NPV; organizational behavior theories such as
Tuckman’s Ladder, Theory X and Theory Y, Maslow's hierarchy of needs; commonly frowned
upon project management practices, such as gold plating; and others.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Physiological needs such as food water and sleep must be met before financial**
compensation, recognition, and social relationships can significantly motivate the team.
Correct. Abraham Maslow grouped motivational factors into a hierarchy, with
physiological needs such as air, food, and water at the lowest and most fundamental level.
Once these essential needs are met, then people are motivated by higher order factors, such
as financial security, recognition, and social acceptance.
- **B All workers fit into two groups, X and Y. The X group avoids responsibility, does the least**
work possible, and requires constant supervision. Those in the Y group are willing to work
without close supervision and want to achieve.
Incorrect. This answer choice describes McGregor's theory of X and Y.
- **C All motivators can be divided into hygiene factors that must be satisfied, such as working**
conditions and salary; and motivating agents such as responsibility and recognition.
Incorrect. This answer choice refers to Herzberg's motivation-hygiene theory.
- **D There are three universal motivators: achievement, affiliation, and power. In every person,**
one of these three will dominate the other two.
Incorrect. This is McClelland's theory of needs.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 318; see
also https://www.pmi.org/learning/library/meet-needs-theories-project-management-4862

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 164 of 200
Question ID: 613633
You are advising a project manager who is new to your company and has just been assigned to
manage a project. The sponsor on his project is very demanding and is asking to see a project
schedule developed as soon as possible. The project manager would like to meet the sponsor's
request and produce a project schedule as quickly as possible but without jeopardizing work
quality.
Which of the following represent the best advice for the project manager in this case?
Top of Form
- **A Develop the activity list, then the WBS and WBS dictionary**
- **B Develop the WBS and activity list concurrently with the help of project team members**
- **C Develop the WBS and activity list concurrently using the project manager's expertise, rather than**
the whole project team
- **D Ask senior management for a new sponsor within the company**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The WBS and WBS dictionary are used as the basis for the development of the final activity list.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The WBS defines the work package deliverables, which are then decomposed into the activities
required to produce those deliverables. Therefore, ideally, the WBS is developed first as part of
the Create WBS process, and the activity list is created later on during the Define Activities
process to which the WBS, a component of the scope baseline, serves as an input. Under certain
circumstances, for example, when the plans are needed urgently as described in this scenario, the

---

project manager may choose to develop the activity list and WBS concurrently. But in such
cases, it is important for the project manager to involve the project team members in the Define
Activities process to ensure better and more accurate results without compromising the quality of
the plans. Therefore, of the choices provided, developing the WBS and activity list concurrently
with the help of project team members is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Develop the activity list, then the WBS and WBS dictionary**
Incorrect. The WBS defines the work package deliverables, which are then decomposed into
the activities required to produce those deliverables. Since the WBS must be developed
before the activity list, this would not be the correct answer choice.
- **B Develop the WBS and activity list concurrently with the help of project team members**
Correct. The activity list and WBS can be developed either sequentially or concurrently, but
the project manager may save a little time by doing them concurrently. It is important to
involve team members in the Define Activities process of decomposition to ensure more
accurate results.
- **C Develop the WBS and activity list concurrently using the project manager's expertise,**
rather than the whole project team
Incorrect. Though it may be tempting to do the work independently to save time, it is
important to involve team members in the Define Activities process. Those closest to the
work will have a better understanding of the effort needed to complete a work package, so
including them in the decomposition of project deliverables will result in a better and more
accurate activities list.
- **D Ask senior management for a new sponsor within the company**
Incorrect. There is not enough information in the question to determine if replacing the
project sponsor would be the best course of action in this case. Replacing the sponsor is an
overreaction that could create serious problems for the project manager. The sponsor
provides support and resources for the project, so taking this course of action could cause
the project to get canceled or the sponsor to find another project manager!

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 184-185

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 165 of 200
Question ID: 651305
- **A project manager must submit various high-level performance reports to executive managers**
throughout the organization. The project team broke down the work to align with the reporting
needs to integrate costs, resources, and scope.
Which level of the WBS should the project manager report?
Top of Form
- **A Work package**
- **B Control account**
- **C Activity list**
- **D Planning package**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How are most work breakdown structures organized?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

- **A typical project work breakdown structure, or WBS, consists of control accounts, work**
packages, and planning packages. The work packages are broken down further into activities.
Among those four components, the one that aligns best with the project manager’s reporting need
is the control accounts. Control accounts are management control points where scope, costs, and
schedule are integrated and measured. This is exactly the high-level reporting needs requested by
the executive managers throughout the organization.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Work package**
Incorrect. A work package is the lowest level of the work breakdown structure. At the work
package level in a company to warrant many executive managers is too detailed and too
isolated to provide meaningful information for their needs. They seek reporting at a high
level, not at a low level.
- **B Control account**
Correct. Managers throughout the project manager’s organization are requesting
performance reports at a high level. They are not seeking the detailed data for low-level
operations and activities. The control accounts integrate the costs, scope, and schedule
points and compare their performance using the earned value management metrics.
- **C Activity list**
Incorrect. Activity lists are created when work packages are decomposed further.
Technically they are not considered part of the work breakdown structure. Nevertheless, the
lists are way too detailed for executive managers to care or make appropriate high-level
decisions, for instance at a program or portfolio management level.
- **D Planning package**
Incorrect. Planning packages represent the work that has not yet been broken down to the
work package level. Some of the information captured in the planning packages may be of
interest to the executive managers, but they do not contain enough detail and content to
report out project performance.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 158-161, 702

PMP Exam 5

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 166 of 200
Question ID: 612160
- **A retailer has an aggressive expansion plan for four new stores. Each of the four projects is led**
by a project manager. The projects are being managed in a coordinated manner. Three of the
stores are ahead of schedule. The fourth store is well behind schedule, and its project manager
wants some construction workers from the other locations to be transferred to help out.
What should the project manager do first to secure the additional workers?
Top of Form
- **A Submit a change request to increase the scope baseline**
- **B Direct the other project managers to provide additional resources**
- **C Capture the information in the lessons learned register**
- **D Escalate the issue to the program manager**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Who has the authority over projects that are being managed as a group?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

- **A program is a group of related projects that are being managed in a coordinated manner to**
obtain benefits not available from managing them individually. The question states that all four
projects and project managers are being managed in a coordinated manner, which implies that a
program manager is leading all four projects. Programs are managed by program managers who
ensure that program benefits are delivered as expected by coordinating the activities of a
program's components. In this scenario, with three projects ahead of schedule and one well
behind, it may make sense for the program manager to reallocate some resources to ensure that

---

all four locations can be opened on time. Therefore, of the available choices, escalating the issue
to the program manager is the best answer.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Submit a change request to increase the scope baseline**
Incorrect. The question does not indicate that the scope for any of the projects is being
increased. A change request may be required in this scenario to update the WBS dictionary
with resources required but not to increase the scope baseline. However, submitting the
change request is not the first thing for the project manager to do. Another answer choice
more accurately addresses the question asked.
- **B Direct the other project managers to provide additional resources**
Incorrect. The four projects and project managers are being managed in a coordinated
manner, which suggests that they are being managed by a program manager. A project
manager is not likely to have authority over the other project managers within a program.
The project manager could discuss the situation with the other project managers but would
not be in a position to direct the other project managers to provide some of their workers.
- **C Capture the information in the lessons learned register**
Incorrect. The reasons behind the project delays may need to be captured in the lessons
learned register to improve the performance of the current and future projects. However,
just capturing the information in the lessons learned register would not secure additional
resources for the project.
- **D Escalate the issue to the program manager**
Correct. The question states that all four projects and project managers are being managed
in a coordinated manner, which implies that a program manager is leading all four
projects. In this situation, it may make sense for the program manager to reallocate some
resources to balance performance among the projects.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 13

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 167 of 200
Question ID: 625112
The following table is taken from the project's current performance report. The current cost
performance is expected to remain unchanged for the remainder of the project. The method used
to determine the earned value is based on percent complete.
Based on this information, what is the VAC for the project?
Top of Form
- **A $500,000**
- **B -$166,667**
- **C $666,667**

---

- **D $166,667**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The formula for the variance at completion is VAC = BAC - EAC. When the cost performance is
expected to be unchanged for the remainder of the project, the EAC can be calculated as BAC /
CPI.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question is asking for the variance at completion (VAC) based on the assumption that the
cost performance will not change for the remainder of the project. The VAC can be calculated as
BAC - EAC, where BAC is the budget at completion, EAC is the estimate at completion. The
BAC for this project is provided as $500,000 (which is shown on the chart as the planned value
for the project). However, the EAC must be calculated. When the cost performance is not
expected to change, as in the scenario described, the EAC can be calculated as BAC / CPI, where
CPI is the cost performance index. The formula for CPI is earned value (EV) divided by actual
costs (AC). The EV is the sum of the planned work completed, which, in this case, is 100% of
activity 1, 100% of activity 2, and 50% of activity 3. AC is the sum of the costs for each of the
individual activities, as provided in the chart. Note, since the scenario mentions that the method
used to determine the earned value is based on percent complete, the earned value of a partially
completed work package is calculated by multiplying the planned value of the work package by
its the percent complete.
The calculations are shown below:
EV = EV of activity 1 + EV of activity 2 + EV of activity 3 = (1 x $15,000) + (1 x $10,000) +
(0.50 x $250,000) = $150,000
AC = AC of activity 1 + AC of activity 2 + AC of activity 3 = $14,000 + $11,000 + $175,000 =
$200,000
CPI = EV / AC = $150,000 / $200,000 = 0.75
EAC = BAC / CPI = $500,000 / 0.75 = $666,667
VAC = BAC - EAC = $500,000 - $666,6667 = -$166,667
Therefore, in this case, the VAC is -$166,667. Since the VAC is negative, the project is running
over planned costs.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A $500,000**
Incorrect. This answer choice represents the budget at completion (BAC) which is the total
planned value of the project. However, the question is asking for the VAC and not the BAC.
- **B -$166,667**
Correct. In order to derive the VAC, the following calculations must be made: EV = (1 x
$15,000) + (1 x $10,000) + (0.50 x $250,000) = $150,000. AC is provided in the chart as
$200,000. Thus, CPI = EV / AC = $150,000 / $200,000 = 0.75. EAC = BAC / CPI =
$500,000 / 0.75 = $666,667. Therefore, VAC = BAC - EAC = $500,000 - $666,6667 =
-$166,667
- **C $666,667**
Incorrect. The value given in this answer choice represents the estimate at completion
(EAC). The EAC for the project can be calculated as BAC / CPI = $500,000 / 0.75 =
$666,667. However, the question is asking for the VAC rather than the EAC.
- **D $166,667**
Incorrect. This answer choice represents a miscalculation of the VAC formula. The formula
for VAC is: VAC = BAC - EAC. If the BAC and EAC are transposed in the formula, then the
result would be $166,667.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 262, 267
Practice Standard for Earned Value Management - Second Edition, Project Management
Institute Inc., 2011, Page(s) 38-39
https://www.project-management-prepcast.com/pmp-formulas

Question 168 of 200
Question ID: 613403
- **A project manager is in the planning stage of a project to construct a new water treatment**
facility. Currently, the project manager is preparing to develop the change management plan. The
performing organization has a project management office (PMO), which can best be described as
supportive.
What role might the PMO play in the development of the change management plan?
Top of Form
- **A The PMO will prepare the change management plan for the project**
- **B A PMO assists with project execution and would not be involved in project planning**
- **C Supply a template for the change management plan**
- **D The project manager reports to the PMO, and the PMO directly manages the project**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might a PMO best support the project manager with the development of the change
management plan?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The change management plan is a component of the project management plan that establishes the
change control board, documents the extent of its authority, and describes how the change
control system will be implemented. A supportive PMO provides a consultative role to projects
by supplying templates, best practices, training, access to information, and lessons learned from

---

other projects. Therefore, of the available choices, supplying a template best describes the role a
supportive PMO might play in the development of the change management plan.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The PMO will prepare the change management plan for the project**
Incorrect. A PMO might supply a template for the change management plan, but it is the
project manager's responsibility to develop the change management plan for the project.
- **B A PMO assists with project execution and would not be involved in project planning**
Incorrect. When an organization utilizes a supportive PMO, the PMO will support the
project throughout the entire project lifecycle and not just project execution.
- **C Supply a template for the change management plan**
Correct. A supportive PMO provides a consultative role to projects by supplying templates,
best practices, training, access to information, and lessons learned from other projects.
- **D The project manager reports to the PMO, and the PMO directly manages the project**
Incorrect. This answer choice describes a directive rather than supportive PMO, and the
question specifies that the PMO can best be described as supportive.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 48, 88, 116

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 169 of 200
Question ID: 612716
- **A project manager is leading a project in which unseasonal weather conditions have caused the**
office building construction project to run well behind schedule.
What could the project manager have done differently earlier in the project to address the
unpredictability of weather conditions?
Top of Form
- **A Pre-assigned team members during project initiation**
- **B Utilized risk exploiting as a risk response strategy**
- **C Developed a cause and effect diagram**
- **D Conducted a Monte Carlo analysis**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What analysis technique would provide a range of possible outcomes for the project?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

- **A variability risk represents an uncertainty, which exists about some key characteristics of a**
planned event, activity, or decision. Unusual weather conditions occurring during the
construction of the office building is an example of a variability risk. A Monte Carlo simulation
is an analysis technique where a computer model is iterated many times, with the input values
chosen at random for each iteration driven by the input data, including probability distributions
and probabilistic branches. Outputs are generated to represent the range of possible outcomes for
the project. Variability risks can be addressed using Monte Carlo analysis, with the range of
variation reflected in probability distributions, followed by actions to reduce the spread of

---

possible outcomes. Therefore, of the available options, conducting a Monte Carlo analysis is the
best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Pre-assigned team members during project initiation**
Incorrect. Pre-assignment is a tool that can be used as part of the Acquire Resources
process to determine project resources, such as team members, in advance. Even if the
project manager had the authority to make pre-assignment, it is unlikely that this action
could have helped the project manager in addressing the unpredictability of weather
conditions.
- **B Utilized risk exploiting as a risk response strategy**
Incorrect. The exploit strategy is where the project team acts to ensure that an opportunity
occurs. However, the question describes a risk, which represents a threat to the project
rather than an opportunity.
- **C Developed a cause and effect diagram**
Incorrect. A cause and effect diagram is a decomposition technique that helps trace an
undesirable effect back to its root cause. A cause and effect diagram is helpful in
understanding the root cause of a problem once it has occurred. The diagram is not likely
to be used to address a risk 'before' it has occurred.
- **D Conducted a Monte Carlo analysis**
Correct. Variability risks can be addressed using Monte Carlo analysis, with the range of
variation reflected in probability distributions, followed by actions to reduce the spread of
possible outcomes.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 398-399
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 170 of 200
Question ID: 613762
You are facilitating a risk workshop with your project team to discuss, evaluate, and prioritize
previously identified project risks based on the probability and impact of each risk. During the
meeting, a key stakeholder proposes that as part of the analysis, the team consider other
characteristics of risk beyond just probability and impact.
Which of the following is the least likely characteristic proposed by the stakeholder:
Top of Form
- **A Dormancy**
- **B Propinquity**
- **C Manageability**
- **D Sensitivity**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which characteristic is considered when creating tornado diagrams as part of the Perform
Quantitative Risk Analysis process?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The scenario describes a risk workshop, a technique used in conducting a qualitative risk
analysis. However, sensitivity analysis is a technique used as part of quantitative risk analysis to
determine which project risks or other sources of uncertainty have the most potential impact on
project outcomes. Also, a sensitivity analysis focuses on evaluating a risk’s potential impact on
achieving project objectives. Since the project stakeholder in this scenario is looking to use the

---

characteristics of risk beyond probability and impact to conduct the analysis, it is reasonable to
assume that sensitivity is the least likely characteristic suggested by the stakeholder.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Dormancy**
Incorrect. Dormancy is one of the characteristics of risk that can be used to prioritize
project risks. It represents the period of time that may elapse after a risk has occurred
before its impact is discovered.
- **B Propinquity**
Incorrect. Propinquity can be defined as “nearness in relationship” and represents the
degree to which something matters personally to an individual stakeholder or a group of
stakeholders. The more a risk is perceived by a stakeholder as being significant,
propinquity is high.
- **C Manageability**
Incorrect. Risks can be assessed and prioritized based on their degree of manageability, or
the ease with which the risk owner can manage the occurrence or impact of a risk.
- **D Sensitivity**
Correct. Sensitivity analysis is a technique used as part of quantitative, not qualitative, risk
analysis to determine which project risks or other sources of uncertainty have the most
potential impact on project outcomes. A sensitivity analysis focuses on evaluating a risk’s
potential impact on achieving project objectives. However, the goal in the scenario
described is to find characteristics of risk to use beyond probability and impact. Therefore,
sensitivity analysis would not be the appropriate technique to use in this situation.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 423-424, 434
