PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 194 of 200
Question ID: 612323
The project manager is having difficulty with recurring conflict among team members who are
self-driven experts in their field. He is looking for an appropriate way to manage them and calls
them to a meeting. He gathers differing perspectives from each team member and through open
dialogue builds consensus and commitment.
What conflict management technique has the project manager used in this situation?
Top of Form
- **A Withdrawing**
- **B Compromising**
- **C Forcing**
- **D Collaborating**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which conflict management technique can result in a win-win situation?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The project manager is using collaboration by incorporating multiple viewpoints and insights
from the differing perspectives through open dialogue to gain consensus and build commitment.
This approach can result in a win-win situation. Of the available answer choices, collaborating is
the best description of the conflict management technique used by the project manager.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Withdrawing**
Incorrect. The project manager took an active role in addressing the issue by conducting a
meeting, rather than withdrawing from the problem.
- **B Compromising**
Incorrect. Compromising is characterized by each side of a dispute making concessions
which bring some satisfaction to all parties to temporarily or partially resolve the conflict.
There is no indication from the question that any concessions have been made to support
this answer choice.
- **C Forcing**
Incorrect. Forcing involves pushing one's viewpoint at the expense of others, which is
inconsistent with the question's characterization of building consensus among the team
members.
- **D Collaborating**
Correct. Collaborating incorporates multiple viewpoints and insights from the differing
perspectives through open dialogue that typically leads to consensus and commitment.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 349

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 195 of 200
Question ID: 610012
- **A supplier requires two months to manufacture the necessary equipment for a project. This**
situation means that the project manager must order the equipment at least two months before the
installation start date.
This dependency is an example of which of the following?
Top of Form
- **A Mandatory logic**
- **B Discretionary dependency**
- **C Hard logic**
- **D Soft logic**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The scenario refers to a dependency that is inherent in the nature of the work.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario refers to a dependency that is inherent in the nature of the work. Mandatory
dependencies are those that are contractually required or inherent in the nature of the work.
Mandatory dependencies are also sometimes referred to as hard logic. Therefore, of the choices
provided, hard logic is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Mandatory logic**
Incorrect. 'Mandatory logic' is a fake term made up for this question.
- **B Discretionary dependency**
Incorrect. Discretionary dependencies are established based on knowledge of best practices
within a particular application area or some unusual aspect of the project where a specific
sequence is desired, even though there may be other acceptable sequences. The scenario
suggests that the dependency is required rather than desired.
- **C Hard logic**
Correct. Mandatory dependencies are those that are contractually required or inherent in
the nature of the work. Mandatory dependencies are also sometimes referred to as hard
logic. Being forced to place the equipment order at least two months before the installation
start date is best described by hard logic.
- **D Soft logic**
Incorrect. Discretionary dependencies are sometimes referred to as preferred logic,
preferential logic, or soft logic. The dependency described by the question is inherent in the
nature of the work. Therefore, the dependency represents a requirement rather than a
preference.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 191

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 196 of 200
Question ID: 612202
You are the project manager for a large healthcare organization managing the installation of an
electronic medical record (EMR) system. The installation requires a lot of different hardware
purchases since this will be the first time an EMR has been used in the organization. You have
been working through the procurement process, and you are now in the Control Procurements
process.
Which of the following activities will you perform as part of that process?
Top of Form
- **A Close contracts with sellers**
- **B Identify potential sellers**
- **C Review sellers' responses**
- **D Perform source selection analysis**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The Control Procurements process occurs after an agreement has been signed and the
deliverables of the seller accepted.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Control Procurements is the process of managing procurement relationships, monitoring contract
performance, and closing out contracts. The scenario is vague as to whether you are ready to
close contracts; it only asks which activities are performed in the Control Procurements process.
It's important to recognize that in the case of procurement management, closing contracts is part
of the processes performed in the Monitoring and Controlling Process Group and not part of the

---

Close Project or Phase process in the Project Integration Management Knowledge Area.
Therefore, closing contracts with sellers is part of Control Procurements and, hence is the correct
answer.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Close contracts with sellers**
Correct. Control Procurements is the process of managing procurement relationships,
monitoring contract performance, and closing out contracts.
- **B Identify potential sellers**
Incorrect. The Plan Procurement Management process is where everything related to
procurements is planned and developed. Make-or-buy decisions, procurement strategy, bid
documents, the procurement statement of work and identifying potential sellers are all
outputs of this process making this an incorrect answer.
- **C Review sellers' responses**
Incorrect. Conduct Procurements is the process of obtaining seller responses, selecting
sellers, and awarding contracts. Therefore, reviewing seller responses would be part of the
Conduct Procurements process and not part of Control Procurements.
- **D Perform source selection analysis**
Incorrect. Source selection analysis is a tool used during Plan Procurement Management to
decide on an evaluation method that will be used for selecting sellers during the Conduct
Procurements process. Since it is used in the selection of sellers and precedes any contract
with sellers, it is not part of the Control Procurements process and an incorrect answer.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 492, 499

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 197 of 200
Question ID: 612294
You have been asked to lead a product development project which will use an agile framework.
Currently, you are in the process of drafting the project charter, and you want to bring together
stakeholders and subject matter experts to discuss perceived project risk, success criteria, and
other topics.
What is the best way for you to accomplish this objective?
Top of Form
- **A Facilitate an iteration retrospective**
- **B Invite the relevant participants to the daily scrum meetings**
- **C Conduct interviews with the identified individuals**
- **D Schedule a focus group**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project charter is developed during project initiation.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question states that the project charter is being drafted which implies that the project is in the
initiation stage. A focus group is a data-gathering technique which may be beneficial in the
development of the project charter. Focus groups bring together stakeholders and subject matter
experts to learn about the perceived project risk, success criteria, and other topics in a more
conversational way than a one-on-one interview. The expectations of the project manager do not
change in an adaptive (agile) environment, but control of the detailed product planning and
delivery is delegated to the team who, in the scenario described, can be considered the subject

---

matter experts. The incorrect answer choices represent meetings that would take place after
project initiation has been completed or are not held in a group setting. Therefore, of the
available choices, scheduling a focus group is the best answer.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Facilitate an iteration retrospective**
Incorrect. An iteration retrospective is a scheduled meeting to gather lessons learned at the
end of an iteration. The question indicates that the project charter is under development as
part of project initiation, and an iteration retrospective would not take place until project
execution is underway.
- **B Invite the relevant participants to the daily scrum meetings**
Incorrect. A daily scrum meeting is a time-boxed meeting held daily to discuss what has
been accomplished since the previous daily scrum, what will be done during the next 24
hours, and to identify any obstacles. A daily scrum meeting is not held to support the
development of the project charter.
- **C Conduct interviews with the identified individuals**
Incorrect. Interviews are used to obtain information from stakeholders by talking to them
directly in a one-on-one setting. Whereas, the question describes a meeting that will be held
as a discussion in a group environment.
- **D Schedule a focus group**
Correct. Focus groups bring together stakeholders and subject matter experts to learn
about the perceived project risk, success criteria, and other topics in a more conversational
way than a one-on-one interview. Of the options provided, a focus group best addresses the
needs described in the scenario.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 80, 74

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 198 of 200
Question ID: 625206
You have been managing a project to launch a new CRM platform for a large retail organization.
After a few weeks into the project, you perform some calculations and determine that the SPI is
0.8 and the CPI is 1.2. Your senior management wants you to get the project back on track.
What is your best course of action in this situation?
Top of Form
- **A Perform resource leveling**
- **B Reduce the scope of the project**
- **C Adjust the schedule baseline**
- **D Crash the schedule**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is the best action to compress the schedule?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The first thing to do is to interpret the values of the SPI and the CPI. The SPI of 0.8 means the
project is behind schedule. The CPI of 1.2 means the project is under budget. Therefore, the
problem that senior management wants to be addressed is the schedule overrun. Ideally, a change
request needs to be submitted before taking any action. However, this option is not provided
among the answer choices. Therefore, crashing the schedule is the best solution under these
circumstances.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Perform resource leveling**
Incorrect. Resource leveling would address an issue of limited resources but may increase
the schedule rather than compress it.
- **B Reduce the scope of the project**
Incorrect. The problem that needs to be addressed is a schedule overrun. Although
reducing scope is an option, there is not enough information provided in the question to
suggest this is the best course of action, especially as a scope reduction would likely reduce
the value provided by the project. The question indicates that the project is behind
schedule. Therefore, the project manager should find a way to compress the schedule.
- **C Adjust the schedule baseline**
Incorrect. Adjusting the schedule baseline cannot be done without submitting a change
request first. Moreover, this answer choice is vague as to what adjustment exactly is
required. Also, the project can be brought back on track without modifying the schedule
baseline, for example, by applying the crashing technique.
- **D Crash the schedule**
Correct. Crashing the schedule is the best solution to the identified problem. Crashing is a
schedule compression technique that will add resources to an activity on the critical path to
shorten the duration. Crashing the schedule will increase costs. However, this solution is
best for a project that is behind schedule and under budget.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 215

Question 199 of 200
Question ID: 612152
- **A manufacturer has initiated a project as the result of a Lean Six Sigma value stream mapping**
exercise of its production process.
In this scenario, which specific factor led to the creation of the project?
Top of Form
- **A Market demand**
- **B Competitive forces**
- **C Business process improvements**
- **D Stakeholder demands**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Value stream mapping is a lean enterprise technique used to document, analyze, and improve the
flow of information or materials required to produce a product or service for a customer.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Value stream mapping is a lean enterprise technique used to document, analyze, and improve the
flow of information or materials required to produce a product or service for a customer. The
question describes a situation where the company has analyzed its production process and
recommended improvements, which can be made with the initiation of a project to realize greater
efficiency. Even though the scenario describes a manufacturing process, the value stream
mapping technique is often used on knowledge projects carried out using the agile framework.

---

An argument can be made that any of the answer choices represent factors that may have played
a role in the decision to move forward with the project. However, a Lean Six Sigma value stream
exercise as it relates to a production process is specifically related to process improvements to
gain greater efficiencies in capital, labor, and/or materials. Therefore, of the available choices,
business process improvements provide the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Market demand**
Incorrect. A change in market demand may drive a company to update their offerings of
products or services. For example, an increase in fuel costs may cause consumers to seek
more fuel-efficient cars. However, the question describes the implementation of process
improvement rather than a response to a change in market demand.
- **B Competitive forces**
Incorrect. The question suggests that a project was initiated to improve the efficiency of a
manufacturing process. Although competitive forces may provide the incentive to improve
the efficiency of a production line, there is another answer choice that more directly
addresses the situation described by the question.
- **C Business process improvements**
Correct. The question describes a situation where the company has analyzed its production
process and recommended improvements, which can be made with the initiation of a project
to realize greater efficiency.
- **D Stakeholder demands**
Incorrect. Stakeholder demand may have been a factor in the decision to undertake the
project, but it is not specifically mentioned in the question. Another answer choice provides
a more direct answer to the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 9

PMP Exam 5
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 200 of 200
Question ID: 612543
- **A project to develop a new smartphone application for use with a popular operating system is**
underway. To penetrate more markets, a change request has been submitted to expand the project
scope to include an additional operating system that would support the application. The members
of the change control board (CCB) are meeting to discuss the request. They are familiar with the
original operating system but do not have experience with the new one.
What is the best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Reject the request since adding support for another operating system represents scope creep**
- **B Invite a programmer with technical knowledge of the new operating system to the meeting**
- **C Reject the request since the CCB lacks experience with the new operating system**
- **D Defer the request until the application for the original operating system is complete**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might the CCB be in a better position to render an informed decision?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

In this scenario, the members of the CCB are not in a position to render an informed decision on
the change request due to a lack of technical expertise with the new operating system. Expert
judgment should be sought in order to make a decision based on the merits of the request.
Inviting a programmer with technical knowledge of the new operating system to the meeting is
an example of seeking expert judgment. Therefore, of the available options, inviting a

---

programmer with technical knowledge of the new operating system to the meeting is the best
answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Reject the request since adding support for another operating system represents scope**
creep
Incorrect. Scope creep refers to the uncontrolled expansion of product or project scope
without adjustments to time, cost, and resources. The question suggests that the Perform
Integrated Change Control process is being performed, which means that the change is
being controlled by the established process.
- **B Invite a programmer with technical knowledge of the new operating system to the meeting**
Correct. This answer choice describes expert judgment. Expert judgment should be sought
to understand the technical aspects of the new operating system in order to render an
informed decision based on the merits of the request.
- **C Reject the request since the CCB lacks experience with the new operating system**
Incorrect. The expansion of the product scope may or may not be a good idea. In order to
properly evaluate the change request, the CCB should seek guidance from an expert that
has the technical expertise necessary to assist the CCB in making an informed decision
regarding the proposed change. Rejecting the request at this point would be a premature
action.
- **D Defer the request until the application for the original operating system is complete**
Incorrect. The deferment of the request may or may not be a good decision in this situation,
but the members of the CCB lack the technical knowledge to make that determination. The
members of the CCB should seek insight from someone that has expertise with the new
operating system in order to make an informed decision.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 118
